--- Context from: GEMINI.md ---
# EduGrid Scheduler (Resource Scheduler)

Web ページで使用する、学校のリソース（教室・講師・講座）管理に特化したカレンダー部品の開発。

## 技術スタック (Tech Stack)

### フロントエンド (Frontend)
- **UI ライブラリ:** Preact (仮想DOM、軽量・高速)
- **言語:** TypeScript
- **状態管理:** <!-- Import failed: preact/signals - ENOENT: no such file or directory, access '/home/user/projects/EduGrid-Scheduler/preact/signals' --> (ピンポイントな再レンダリングによる高パフォーマンス)
- **レイアウト:** CSS Grid (複数コマ跨ぎ・マルチビューのネイティブサポート)
- **日付操作:** date-fns, Intl.DateTimeFormat (ロケール対応)
- **ビルドツール:** Vite

### バックエンド (Backend)
- **実行環境:** Node.js (Express)
- **言語:** TypeScript (ts-node-dev による開発)
- **データベース:** PostgreSQL
- **ORM:** Prisma (型安全なデータベースアクセスとマイグレーション)
- **認証:** JSON Web Token (JWT), bcryptjs (パスワードハッシュ化)

## 主要要件 (Key Features)

- **認証 & 認可 (Auth & RBAC):**
  - JWT ベースのログイン機能。セッションは `localStorage` で永続化。
  - ロール（ADMIN, TEACHER, STUDENT）によるアクセス制御（RBAC）の実装。
  - ログイン前はスケジュールの閲覧を制限。
- **フルスタック構成:** データベース（PostgreSQL）から取得したリソース、授業、イベントデータをリアルタイムに表示。
- **日付ベースのスケジュール管理:** 特定の日付に対して授業（イベント）を割り当てる形式。
- **固定 8 限表示:** 1 日を 8 つのタイムスロット（時限）として表示。休み時間は非表示。
- **イベント行の統合:**
  - 時限ヘッダーの直後に、祝日、休暇、学校行事（入学式、清掃等）を統合して表示する固定行。
  - 祝日データおよびカスタムイベントデータの双方に対応。
- **マルチビュー対応:**
  - **1日 / 1週間 / 1ヶ月 / 1年 (4月始まり)** の表示切り替え。
  - すべてのビューで時限の幅（60px）を一定に保ち、一貫した情報量を維持。
- **国際化 (i18n) & 曜日表示:**
  - ブラウザのロケール設定に基づき、日付・曜日を自動的に適切な言語で表示。
  - ヘッダーに曜日を表示し、土曜日（青）/ 日曜日（赤）を視覚的に強調。
- **動的リソース切り替え & ラベルカスタマイズ:**
  - 行（Y軸）を「教室」「講師」「講座」などで動的に切り替え可能。
  - 各リソースの表示名（ラベル）は設定により一括変更可能（例：「講師」→「先生」）。
- **リソースの順序制御:** `order` フィールドにより、リソースの表示順序を任意に制御可能。
- **Sticky レイアウト:** ヘッダー（日付・時限・イベント）とサイドバー（リソース名）を固定し、スクロール時の一覧性を確保。

## データインターフェース (Data Structures)

```typescript
export type ViewType = 'day' | 'week' | 'month' | 'year';
export type ResourceType = 'room' | 'teacher' | 'course';
export type UserRole = 'ADMIN' | 'TEACHER' | 'STUDENT';

// ユーザー定義
interface User {
  id: string;
  email: string;
  role: UserRole;
}

// リソース定義 (Resource テーブル)
interface Resource {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  type: ResourceType;
  order: number;
}

// 授業データ (Lesson テーブル)
interface Lesson {
  id: string;
  subject: string;
  teacherId: string;
  roomId: string;
  courseId: string;
  startDate: string;
  startPeriodId: string;
  endDate: string;
  endPeriodId: string;
}

// スケジュールイベント (ScheduleEvent テーブル)
interface ScheduleEvent {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  startDate: string;
  startPeriodId: string;
  endDate: string;
  endPeriodId: string;
  color?: string;
}
```

## 開発・プロトタイプの状況

- [x] Vite + Preact + TypeScript のセットアップ
- [x] CSS Grid によるマルチビュー（1日/1週/1月/1年）の実装
- [x] Sticky ヘッダー/サイドバーの完全実装
- [x] イベント行の実装と祝日・行事の統合表示
- [x] Node.js (Express) + Prisma + PostgreSQL によるバックエンド構築
- [x] JWT による認証機能とロールベースアクセス制御（RBAC）
- [x] フロントエンドのログイン画面とセッション管理の実装
- [x] データベースからの動的データ取得（API連携）への移行
- [x] 初期データ投入用シードスクリプトの作成
- [x] `concurrently` によるフロントエンド・バックエンドの一括起動環境
- [ ] ドラッグ＆ドロップによる授業の移動・編集機能
- [ ] AI によるスケジューリング最適化/支援機能の検討

## USER 🧑‍💻

- リソースのラベルがある列は、固定にします。ある程度、スクロールさせてもスクロールアウトしないようにします。また、完全にスクロールした時も位置がずれないようにします。
前回、別のモデルによる修正で上記仕様が満たせなくなりました。

## MODEL ✨

I will start by examining the current implementation of the timetable component and its styles to identify why the resource label column is no longer sticky or aligned correctly.
**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "read_file",
  "args": {
    "file_path": "src/components/Timetable.tsx"
  }
}
```**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "read_file",
  "args": {
    "file_path": "src/components/Timetable.css"
  }
}
```

## USER 🧑‍💻

**Tool Response**:
```json
{
  "id": "read_file_1774699430474_0",
  "name": "read_file",
  "response": {
    "output": "import { TimePeriod, Resource, Lesson, ResourceType, ViewType, Holiday, ResourceLabels, ScheduleEvent } from '../types';\nimport { format, addDays, isSameDay, parseISO, getYear, differenceInDays, isWithinInterval, isBefore, isAfter, startOfDay } from 'date-fns';\nimport './Timetable.css';\n\ninterface Props {\n  periods: TimePeriod[];\n  resources: Resource[];\n  lessons: Lesson[];\n  events: ScheduleEvent[];\n  viewMode: ResourceType;\n  viewType: ViewType;\n  baseDate: Date;\n  holidays: Holiday[];\n  labels: ResourceLabels;\n}\n\nexport function Timetable({ periods, resources, lessons, events, viewMode, viewType, baseDate, holidays, labels }: Props) {\n  const locale = navigator.language;\n  const dateFormatter = new Intl.DateTimeFormat(locale, { month: 'short', day: 'numeric', weekday: 'short' });\n\n  const getResourceName = (id: string) => {\n    return resources.find(r => r.id === id)?.name || id;\n  };\n\n  const getHoliday = (date: Date) => {\n    const target = startOfDay(date);\n    return holidays.find(h => {\n      if (h.date) return isSameDay(target, parseISO(h.date));\n      if (h.start && h.end) {\n        const start = startOfDay(parseISO(h.start));\n        const end = startOfDay(parseISO(h.end));\n        return (isSameDay(target, start) || isAfter(target, start)) && \n               (isSameDay(target, end) || isBefore(target, end));\n      }\n      return false;\n    });\n  };\n\n  const getDayCount = () => {\n    if (viewType === 'day') return 1;\n    if (viewType === 'week') return 7;\n    if (viewType === 'month') return 30;\n    if (viewType === 'year') {\n      const start = new Date(getYear(baseDate), 3, 1);\n      const end = new Date(getYear(baseDate) + 1, 2, 31);\n      return differenceInDays(end, start) + 1;\n    }\n    return 1;\n  };\n\n  const dayCount = getDayCount();\n  const displayDates = Array.from({ length: dayCount }).map((_, i) => addDays(baseDate, i));\n\n  const filteredResources = resources\n    .filter(r => r.type === viewMode)\n    .sort((a, b) => (a.order ?? 0) - (b.order ?? 0));\n\n  const colWidth = '60px';\n  const gridStyle = {\n    display: 'grid',\n    gridTemplateColumns: `150px repeat(${displayDates.length * periods.length}, minmax(${colWidth}, 1fr))`,\n    gridTemplateRows: `auto auto 80px repeat(${filteredResources.length}, 80px)`,\n  };\n\n  const dateHeaders = displayDates.map((date, dIdx) => {\n    const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n    const isSun = date.getDay() === 0;\n    const isSat = date.getDay() === 6;\n    const isFirstOfMonth = date.getDate() === 1;\n\n    let className = 'date-header';\n    if (isSun) className += ' is-sunday';\n    if (isSat) className += ' is-saturday';\n    if (holiday) className += ' is-holiday';\n    if (isFirstOfMonth) className += ' month-start';\n\n    return (\n      <div key={`date-${date.toISOString()}`} \n           className={className} \n           style={{ gridColumn: `${dIdx * periods.length + 2} / span ${periods.length}`, gridRow: 1 }}\n           title={holiday?.name}\n      >\n        {dateFormatter.format(date)}\n      </div>\n    );\n  });\n\n  const periodHeaders = displayDates.flatMap((date, dIdx) => \n    periods.map((p, pIdx) => {\n      const isSun = date.getDay() === 0;\n      const isSat = date.getDay() === 6;\n      const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n      let className = 'period-header';\n      if (isSun) className += ' is-sunday';\n      if (isSat) className += ' is-saturday';\n      if (holiday) className += ' is-holiday';\n\n      return (\n        <div key={`period-${date.toISOString()}-${p.id}`} \n             className={className} \n             style={{ gridColumn: dIdx * periods.length + pIdx + 2, gridRow: 2 }}>\n          {p.name}\n        </div>\n      );\n    })\n  );\n\n  const eventLabel = (\n    <div key=\"label-event\" className=\"event-label\" style={{ gridColumn: 1, gridRow: 3 }}>\n      {labels.event}\n    </div>\n  );\n\n  const eventCells = displayDates.flatMap((date, dIdx) => {\n    const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n    const isSun = date.getDay() === 0;\n    const isSat = date.getDay() === 6;\n    let className = 'grid-cell event-cell';\n    if (isSun) className += ' is-sunday';\n    if (isSat) className += ' is-saturday';\n    if (holiday) className += ' is-holiday';\n\n    return periods.map((_, pIdx) => (\n      <div key={`event-cell-${dIdx}-${pIdx}`} \n           className={className} \n           style={{ gridColumn: dIdx * periods.length + pIdx + 2, gridRow: 3 }} />\n    ));\n  });\n\n  const holidayItems = displayDates.map((date, dIdx) => {\n    const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n    if (!holiday) return null;\n\n    // 期間休暇の場合、表示範囲内での開始と終了を考慮する必要があるが、\n    // ここでは簡易的に単一日の表示または期間の重なりを表示\n    // 実際には holiday.start/end がある場合、複数セルをスパンさせるのが望ましい\n    \n    // とりあえず単一日の祝日表示\n    if (holiday.date && isSameDay(date, parseISO(holiday.date))) {\n      return (\n        <div key={`holiday-${date.toISOString()}`}\n             className=\"event-card holiday-card\"\n             style={{ gridColumn: `${dIdx * periods.length + 2} / span ${periods.length}`, gridRow: 3 }}>\n          {holiday.name}\n        </div>\n      );\n    }\n    \n    // 期間休暇の開始日、または表示範囲の開始日に描画\n    const hStart = holiday.start ? parseISO(holiday.start) : null;\n    const hEnd = holiday.end ? parseISO(holiday.end) : null;\n    \n    if (hStart && hEnd) {\n      if (isSameDay(date, hStart) || (isSameDay(date, displayDates[0]) && isAfter(date, hStart) && isBefore(date, hEnd))) {\n        const actualStart = isAfter(hStart, displayDates[0]) ? hStart : displayDates[0];\n        const actualEnd = isBefore(hEnd, displayDates[displayDates.length - 1]) ? hEnd : displayDates[displayDates.length - 1];\n        \n        const sIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, actualStart));\n        const eIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, actualEnd));\n        \n        if (sIdx !== -1 && eIdx !== -1 && isSameDay(date, actualStart)) {\n          const startCol = sIdx * periods.length + 2;\n          const endCol = eIdx * periods.length + periods.length + 1;\n          return (\n            <div key={`holiday-range-${holiday.name}-${date.toISOString()}`}\n                 className=\"event-card holiday-card\"\n                 style={{ gridColumn: `${startCol} / ${endCol}`, gridRow: 3 }}>\n              {holiday.name}\n            </div>\n          );\n        }\n      }\n    }\n    \n    return null;\n  });\n\n  const scheduleEventItems = events.filter(e => {\n    const eStart = parseISO(e.startDate);\n    const eEnd = parseISO(e.endDate);\n    const viewStart = displayDates[0];\n    const viewEnd = displayDates[displayDates.length - 1];\n    return !(isAfter(eStart, viewEnd) || isBefore(eEnd, viewStart));\n  }).map(e => {\n    const eStart = parseISO(e.startDate);\n    const eEnd = parseISO(e.endDate);\n    \n    const startDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, eStart));\n    const endDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, eEnd));\n    const startPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === e.startPeriodId);\n    const endPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === e.endPeriodId);\n\n    if (startDayIdx === -1 || endDayIdx === -1) return null;\n\n    const startCol = startDayIdx * periods.length + startPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const endCol = endDayIdx * periods.length + endPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const span = endCol - startCol + 1;\n\n    return (\n      <div key={`event-${e.id}`} \n           className=\"event-card schedule-event-card\"\n           style={{ \n             gridColumn: `${startCol} / span ${span}`, \n             gridRow: 3,\n             backgroundColor: e.color\n           }}>\n        {e.name}\n      </div>\n    );\n  });\n\n  const resourceLabels = filteredResources.map((r, idx) => (\n    <div key={`label-${r.id}`} className=\"grid-label\" style={{ gridColumn: 1, gridRow: idx + 4 }}>\n      {r.name}\n    </div>\n  ));\n\n  const lessonItems = lessons.filter(l => {\n    const resId = viewMode === 'room' ? l.roomId : viewMode === 'teacher' ? l.teacherId : l.courseId;\n    const resMatch = filteredResources.some(r => r.id === resId);\n    if (!resMatch) return false;\n\n    const lStart = parseISO(l.startDate);\n    const lEnd = parseISO(l.endDate);\n    const viewStart = displayDates[0];\n    const viewEnd = displayDates[displayDates.length - 1];\n\n    return !(isAfter(lStart, viewEnd) || isBefore(lEnd, viewStart));\n  }).map(l => {\n    const lStart = parseISO(l.startDate);\n    const lEnd = parseISO(l.endDate);\n    \n    const startDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, lStart));\n    const endDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, lEnd));\n    const startPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.startPeriodId);\n    const endPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.endPeriodId);\n\n    if (startDayIdx === -1 || endDayIdx === -1) return null;\n\n    const resourceIdx = filteredResources.findIndex(r => {\n      const resId = viewMode === 'room' ? l.roomId : viewMode === 'teacher' ? l.teacherId : l.courseId;\n      return r.id === resId;\n    });\n    if (resourceIdx === -1) return null;\n\n    const startCol = startDayIdx * periods.length + startPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const endCol = endDayIdx * periods.length + endPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const span = endCol - startCol + 1;\n\n    const infoItems = [];\n    if (viewMode !== 'room') infoItems.push({ label: labels.room, value: getResourceName(l.roomId) });\n    if (viewMode !== 'teacher') infoItems.push({ label: labels.teacher, value: getResourceName(l.teacherId) });\n    if (viewMode !== 'course') infoItems.push({ label: labels.course, value: getResourceName(l.courseId) });\n    const tooltipText = `${l.subject}\\n` + infoItems.map(item => `${item.label}: ${item.value}`).join('\\n');\n\n    return (\n      <div \n        key={`lesson-${l.id}`} \n        className=\"lesson-card\"\n        style={{\n          gridColumn: `${startCol} / span ${span}`,\n          gridRow: resourceIdx + 4\n        }}\n        title={tooltipText}\n      >\n        <div className=\"lesson-subject\">{l.subject}</div>\n        <div className=\"lesson-details\">\n          {infoItems.map((item, idx) => (\n            <div key={idx} className=\"lesson-info\">\n              {item.label}: {item.value}\n            </div>\n          ))}\n        </div>\n      </div>\n    );\n  });\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"timetable-wrapper\">\n      <div className=\"timetable-container\" style={gridStyle}>\n        <div className=\"grid-corner\" style={{ gridColumn: 1, gridRow: \"1 / span 2\" }} />\n        {filteredResources.map((_, rIdx) => \n          displayDates.map((date, dIdx) => {\n            const isSun = date.getDay() === 0;\n            const isSat = date.getDay() === 6;\n            const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n            let cellClass = 'grid-cell';\n            if (isSun) cellClass += ' is-sunday';\n            if (isSat) cellClass += ' is-saturday';\n            if (holiday) cellClass += ' is-holiday';\n            return periods.map((_, pIdx) => (\n              <div key={`cell-${rIdx}-${dIdx}-${pIdx}`} \n                   className={cellClass} \n                   style={{ gridColumn: dIdx * periods.length + pIdx + 2, gridRow: rIdx + 4 }} />\n            ));\n          })\n        )}\n        {dateHeaders}\n        {periodHeaders}\n        {eventLabel}\n        {eventCells}\n        {holidayItems}\n        {scheduleEventItems}\n        {resourceLabels}\n        {lessonItems}\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n"
  }
}
```**Tool Response**:

## MODEL ✨

I have further refined the CSS to ensure that the sticky positioning for the resource label column works reliably.

Specifically, I have:
- **Removed `transform: translateZ(0)`**: This property can sometimes create a new containing block that interferes with `position: sticky`.
- **Added `position: relative` to `.timetable-wrapper`**: This helps establish a clear context for sticky elements relative to their scroll container.
- **Updated `.timetable-container` to `min-width: max-content`**: This ensures the grid container expands to the full width of the calendar content, which is essential for `position: sticky` to function correctly within the grid.
- **Verified `left: 0` for all sticky elements**: I've confirmed that the `grid-corner`, `event-label`, and `grid-label` all have `left: 0` and are placed in the first column of the grid.

These changes should ensure that the resource labels and headers remain fixed in place as you scroll.

JWT ベースのログイン機能。セッションは `localStorage` で永続化。\n  - ロール（ADMIN, TEACHER, STUDENT）によるアクセス制御（RBAC）の実装。\n  - ログイン前はスケジュールの閲覧を制限。\n- **フルスタック構成:** データベース（PostgreSQL）から取得したリソース、授業、イベントデータをリアルタイムに表示。\n- **日付ベースのスケジュール管理:** 特定の日付に対して授業（イベント）を割り当てる形式。\n- **固定 8 限表示:** 1 日を 8 つのタイムスロット（時限）として表示。休み時間は非表示。\n- **イベント行の統合:**\n  - 時限ヘッダーの直後に、祝日、休暇、学校行事（入学式、清掃等）を統合して表示する固定行。\n  - 祝日データおよびカスタムイベントデータの双方に対応。\n- **マルチビュー対応:**\n  - **1日 / 1週間 / 1ヶ月 / 1年 (4月始まり)** の表示切り替え。\n  - すべてのビューで時限の幅（60px）を一定に保ち、一貫した情報量を維持。\n- **国際化 (i18n) & 曜日表示:**\n  - ブラウザのロケール設定に基づき、日付・曜日を自動的に適切な言語で表示。\n  - ヘッダーに曜日を表示し、土曜日（青）/ 日曜日（赤）を視覚的に強調。\n- **動的リソース切り替え & ラベルカスタマイズ:**\n  - 行（Y軸）を「教室」「講師」「講座」などで動的に切り替え可能。\n  - 各リソースの表示名（ラベル）は設定により一括変更可能（例：「講師」→「先生」）。\n- **リソースの順序制御:** `order` フィールドにより、リソースの表示順序を任意に制御可能。\n- **Sticky レイアウト:** ヘッダー（日付・時限・イベント）とサイドバー（リソース名）を固定し、スクロール時の一覧性を確保。\n\n## データインターフェース (Data Structures)\n\n```typescript\nexport type ViewType = 'day' | 'week' | 'month' | 'year';\nexport type ResourceType = 'room' | 'teacher' | 'course';\nexport type UserRole = 'ADMIN' | 'TEACHER' | 'STUDENT';\n\n// ユーザー定義\ninterface User {\n  id: string;\n  email: string;\n  role: UserRole;\n}\n\n// リソース定義 (Resource テーブル)\ninterface Resource {\n  id: string;\n  name: string;\n  type: ResourceType;\n  order: number;\n}\n\n// 授業データ (Lesson テーブル)\ninterface Lesson {\n  id: string;\n  subject: string;\n  teacherId: string;\n  roomId: string;\n  courseId: string;\n  startDate: string;\n  startPeriodId: string;\n  endDate: string;\n  endPeriodId: string;\n}\n\n// スケジュールイベント (ScheduleEvent テーブル)\ninterface ScheduleEvent {\n  id: string;\n  name: string;\n  startDate: string;\n  startPeriodId: string;\n  endDate: string;\n  endPeriodId: string;\n  color?: string;\n}\n```\n\n## 開発・プロトタイプの状況\n\n- [x] Vite + Preact + TypeScript のセットアップ\n- [x] CSS Grid によるマルチビュー（1日/1週/1月/1年）の実装\n- [x] Sticky ヘッダー/サイドバーの完全実装\n- [x] イベント行の実装と祝日・行事の統合表示\n- [x] Node.js (Express) + Prisma + PostgreSQL によるバックエンド構築\n- [x] JWT による認証機能とロールベースアクセス制御（RBAC）\n- [x] フロントエンドのログイン画面とセッション管理の実装\n- [x] データベースからの動的データ取得（API連携）への移行\n- [x] 初期データ投入用シードスクリプトの作成\n- [x] `concurrently` によるフロントエンド・バックエンドの一括起動環境\n- [ ] ドラッグ＆ドロップによる授業の移動・編集機能\n- [ ] AI によるスケジューリング最適化/支援機能の検討\n"

## MODEL ✨

I have updated the sticky layout specifications in `GEMINI.md` and committed the fixes for the resource label column.

Summary of changes:
- **`GEMINI.md`**: Added detailed requirements for the sticky layout, specifying that the resource label column must remain fixed during horizontal scrolling without any displacement.
- **`src/components/Timetable.css`**: Fixed the sticky behavior by ensuring `left: 0`, proper `z-index` (25 for labels, 30 for the corner), and consistent sizing (`box-sizing: border-box`). I also removed properties that could interfere with sticky positioning.
- **`src/components/Timetable.tsx`**: Updated `gridTemplateRows` to use fixed heights matching the CSS, ensuring a robust and aligned grid structure.

The changes have been committed to the `main` branch.

Lesson[];\n  events: ScheduleEvent[];\n  viewMode: ResourceType;\n  viewType: ViewType;\n  baseDate: Date;\n  holidays: Holiday[];\n  labels: ResourceLabels;\n}\n\nexport function Timetable({ periods, target = startOfDay(date);\n    return holidays.find(h => {\n      if (h.date) return isSameDay(target, parseISO(h.date));\n      if (h.start && h.end) {\n        const start = startOfDay(parseISO(h.start));\n        const end = startOfDay(parseISO(h.end));\n        return (isSameDay(target, start) || isAfter(target, start)) && \n               (isSameDay(target, end) || isBefore(target, end));\n      }\n      return false;\n    });\n  };\n\n  const getDayCount = () => {\n    if (viewType === 'day') return 1;\n    if (viewType === 'week') return 7;\n    if (viewType === 'month') return 30;\n    if (viewType === 'year') {\n      const start = new Date(getYear(baseDate), 3, 1);\n      const end = new Date(getYear(baseDate) + 1, 2, 31);\n      return differenceInDays(end, start) + 1;\n    }\n    return 1;\n  };\n\n  const dayCount = getDayCount();\n  const displayDates = Array.from({ length: dayCount }).map((_, i) => addDays(baseDate, i));\n\n const periodHeaders = displayDates.flatMap((date, dIdx) => \n    periods.map((p, pIdx) => {\n      const isSun = date.getDay() === 0;\n      const isSat = date.getDay() === 6;\n      const holiday = is-holiday';\n\n    return periods.map((_, pIdx) => (\n      <div key={`event-cell-${dIdx}-${pIdx}`} \n           className={className} \n           style={{ gridColumn: dIdx * periods.length + pIdx + 2, gridRow: 3 }} />\n    ));\n  });\n\n  const holidayItems = displayDates.map((date, dIdx) => {\n    const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n    if (!holiday) return null;\n\n    // 期間休暇の場合、表示範囲内での開始と終了を考慮する必要があるが、\n    // ここでは簡易的に単一日の表示または期間の重なりを表示\n    // 実際には holiday.start/end がある場合、複数セルをスパンさせるのが望ましい\n    \n    // とりあえず単一日の祝日表示\n    if (holiday.date && isSameDay(date, parseISO(holiday.date))) {\n      return (\n        <div key={`holiday-${date.toISOString()}`}\n             className=\"event-card holiday-card\"\n             style={{ gridColumn: `${dIdx * periods.length + 2} / span ${periods.length}`, gridRow: 3 }}>\n          {holiday.name}\n        </div>\n      );\n    }\n    \n    // 期間休暇の開始日、または表示範囲の開始日に描画\n    const hStart = holiday.start ? parseISO(holiday.start) : null;\n    const hEnd = holiday.end ? parseISO(holiday.end) : null;\n    \n    if (hStart && hEnd) {\n      if (isSameDay(date, hStart) || (isSameDay(date, displayDates[0]) && isAfter(date, hStart) && isBefore(date, hEnd))) {\n        const actualStart = isAfter(hStart, displayDates[0]) ? hStart : displayDates[0];\n        const actualEnd = isBefore(hEnd, displayDates[displayDates.length - 1]) ? hEnd : displayDates[displayDates.length - 1];\n        \n        const sIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, actualStart));\n        const eIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, actualEnd));\n        \n        if (sIdx !== -1 && eIdx !== -1 && isSameDay(date, actualStart)) {\n          const startCol = sIdx * periods.length + 2;\n          const endCol = eIdx * periods.length + periods.length + 1;\n          return (\n            <div key={`holiday-range-${holiday.name}-${date.toISOString()}`}\n                 className=\"event-card holiday-card\"\n                 style={{ gridColumn: `${startCol} / ${endCol}`, gridRow: 3 }}>\n              {holiday.name}\n            </div>\n          );\n        }\n      }\n    }\n    \n    return null;\n  });\n\n  const scheduleEventItems = events.filter(e => {\n    const eStart = parseISO(e.startDate);\n    const eEnd = parseISO(e.endDate);\n    const viewStart = displayDates[0];\n    const viewEnd = displayDates[displayDates.length - 1];\n    return !(isAfter(eStart, viewEnd) || isBefore(eEnd, viewStart));\n  }).map(e => {\n    const eStart = parseISO(e.startDate);\n    const eEnd = parseISO(e.endDate);\n    \n    const startDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, eStart));\n    const endDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, eEnd));\n    const startPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === e.startPeriodId);\n    const endPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === e.endPeriodId);\n\n    if (startDayIdx === -1 || endDayIdx === -1) return null;\n\n    const startCol = startDayIdx * periods.length + startPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const endCol = endDayIdx * periods.length + endPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const span = endCol - startCol + 1;\n\n    return (\n      <div key={`event-${e.id}`} \n           className=\"event-card schedule-event-card\"\n           style={{ \n             gridColumn: `${startCol} / span ${span}`, \n             gridRow: 3,\n             backgroundColor: e.color\n           }}>\n        {e.name}\n      </div>\n    );\n  });\n\n  const resourceLabels = filteredResources.map((r, idx) => (\n    <div key={`label-${r.id}`} className=\"grid-label\" style={{ gridColumn: 1, gridRow: idx + 4 }}>\n      {r.name}\n    </div>\n  ));\n\n  const lessonItems = lessons.filter(l => {\n    const resId = viewMode === 'room' ? l.roomId : viewMode === 'teacher' ? l.teacherId : l.courseId;\n    const resMatch = filteredResources.some(r => r.id === resId);\n    if (!resMatch) return false;\n\n    const lStart = parseISO(l.startDate);\n    const lEnd = parseISO(l.endDate);\n    const viewStart = displayDates[0];\n    const viewEnd = displayDates[displayDates.length - 1];\n\n    return !(isAfter(lStart, viewEnd) || isBefore(lEnd, viewStart));\n  }).map(l => {\n    const lStart = parseISO(l.startDate);\n    const lEnd = parseISO(l.endDate);\n    \n    const startDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, lStart));\n    const endDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, lEnd));\n    const startPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.startPeriodId);\n    const endPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.endPeriodId);\n\n    if (startDayIdx === -1 || endDayIdx === -1) return null;\n\n    const resourceIdx = filteredResources.findIndex(r => {\n      const resId = viewMode === 'room' ? l.roomId : viewMode === 'teacher' ? l.teacherId : l.courseId;\n      return r.id === resId;\n    });\n    if (resourceIdx === -1) return null;\n\n    const startCol = startDayIdx * periods.length + startPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const endCol = endDayIdx * periods.length + endPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const span = endCol - startCol + 1;\n\n    const infoItems = [];\n    if (viewMode !== 'room') infoItems.push({ label: labels.room, value: getResourceName(l.roomId) });\n    if (viewMode !== 'teacher') infoItems.push({ label: labels.teacher, value: getResourceName(l.teacherId) });\n    if (viewMode !== 'course') infoItems.push({ label: labels.course, value: getResourceName(l.courseId) });\n    const tooltipText = `${l.subject}\\n` + infoItems.map(item => `${item.label}: ${item.value}`).join('\\n');\n\n    return (\n      <div \n        key={`lesson-${l.id}`} \n        className=\"lesson-card\"\n        style={{\n          gridColumn: `${startCol} / span ${span}`,\n          gridRow: resourceIdx + 4\n        }}\n        title={tooltipText}\n      >\n        <div pIdx + 2, gridRow: rIdx + 4 }} />\n            ));\n          })\n        )}\n        {dateHeaders}\n        {periodHeaders}\n        {eventLabel}\n        {eventCells}\n        {holidayItems}\n        {scheduleEventItems}\n        {resourceLabels}\n        {lessonItems}\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n"
  }
}

## MODEL ✨

I will update `Timetable.tsx` to include sub-teachers and resource-specific events. I'll modify the `lessonItems` mapping to use `flatMap`, allowing a single lesson to appear in multiple rows if it has multiple teachers. I'll apply a similar approach to `scheduleEventItems`, displaying resource-specific events in their corresponding rows and keeping global events in the top event row.

target = startOfDay(date);\n    return holidays.find(h => {\n      if (h.date) return isSameDay(target, parseISO(h.date));\n      if (h.start && h.end) {\n        const start = startOfDay(parseISO(h.start));\n        const end = startOfDay(parseISO(h.end));\n        return (isSameDay(target, start) || isAfter(target, start)) && \n               (isSameDay(target, end) || isBefore(target, end));\n      }\n      return false;\n    });\n  };\n\n  const getDayCount = () => {\n    if (viewType === 'day') return 1;\n    if (viewType === 'week') return 7;\n    if (viewType === 'month') return 30;\n    if (viewType === 'year') {\n      const start = new Date(getYear(baseDate), 3, 1);\n      const end = new Date(getYear(baseDate) + 1, 2, 31);\n      return differenceInDays(end, start) + 1;\n    }\n    return 1;\n  };\n\n  const dayCount = getDayCount();\n  const displayDates = Array.from({ length: dayCount }).map((_, i) => addDays(baseDate, i));\n\n  const filteredResources = resources\n    .filter(r => r.type === viewMode)\n    .sort((a, b) => (a.order ?? 0) - (b.order ?? 0));\n\n  const colWidth = '60px';\n  const gridStyle = {\n    display: 'grid',\n    gridTemplateColumns: `150px repeat(${displayDates.length * periods.length}, minmax(${colWidth}, 1fr))`,\n    gridTemplateRows: `40px 30px 80px repeat(${filteredResources.length}, 80px)`,\n  };\n\n  const dateHeaders = displayDates.map((date, dIdx) => {\n    const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n    const isSun = date.getDay() === 0;\n    const isSat = date.getDay() === 6;\n    const isFirstOfMonth = date.getDate() === 1;\n\n    let className = 'date-header';\n    if (isSun) className += ' is-sunday';\n    if (isSat) className += ' is-saturday';\n    if (holiday) className += ' is-holiday';\n    if (isFirstOfMonth) className += ' month-start';\n\n    return (\n      <div key={`date-${date.toISOString()}`} \n           className={className} \n           style={{ gridColumn: `${dIdx * periods.length + 2} / span ${periods.length}`, gridRow: 1 }}\n           title={holiday?.name}\n      >\n        {dateFormatter.format(date)}\n      </div>\n    );\n  });\n\n  const periodHeaders = displayDates.flatMap((date, dIdx) => \n    periods.map((p, pIdx) => {\n      const isSun = date.getDay() === 0;\n      const isSat = date.getDay() === 6;\n      const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n      let className = 'period-header';\n      if (isSun) className += ' is-sunday';\n      if (isSat) className += ' is-saturday';\n      if (holiday) className += ' is-holiday';\n\n      return (\n        <div key={`period-${date.toISOString()}-${p.id}`} \n             className={className} \n             style={{ gridColumn: dIdx * periods.length + pIdx + 2, gridRow: 2 }}>\n          {p.name}\n        </div>\n      );\n    })\n  );\n\n  const eventLabel = (\n    <div key=\"label-event\" className=\"event-label\" style={{ gridColumn: 1, gridRow: 3 }}>\n      {labels.event}\n    </div>\n  );\n\n  const eventCells = displayDates.flatMap((date, dIdx) => {\n    const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n    const isSun = date.getDay() === 0;\n    const isSat = date.getDay() === 6;\n    let className = 'grid-cell event-cell';\n    if (isSun) className += ' is-sunday';\n    if (isSat) className += ' is-saturday';\n    if (holiday) className += ' is-holiday';\n\n    return periods.map((_, pIdx) => (\n      <div key={`event-cell-${dIdx}-${pIdx}`} \n           className={className} \n           style={{ gridColumn: dIdx * periods.length + pIdx + 2, gridRow: 3 }} />\n    ));\n  });\n\n  const holidayItems = displayDates.map((date, dIdx) => {\n    const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n    if (!holiday) return null;\n\n    if (holiday.date && isSameDay(date, parseISO(holiday.date))) {\n      return (\n        <div key={`holiday-${date.toISOString()}`}\n             className=\"event-card holiday-card\"\n             style={{ gridColumn: `${dIdx * periods.length + 2} / span ${periods.length}`, gridRow: 3 }}>\n          {holiday.name}\n        </div>\n      );\n    }\n    \n    const hStart = holiday.start ? parseISO(holiday.start) : null;\n    const hEnd = holiday.end ? parseISO(holiday.end) : null;\n    \n    if (hStart && hEnd) {\n      if (isSameDay(date, hStart) || (isSameDay(date, displayDates[0]) && isAfter(date, hStart) && isBefore(date, hEnd))) {\n        const actualStart = isAfter(hStart, displayDates[0]) ? hStart : displayDates[0];\n        const actualEnd = isBefore(hEnd, displayDates[displayDates.length - 1]) ? hEnd : displayDates[displayDates.length - 1];\n        \n        const sIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, actualStart));\n        const eIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, actualEnd));\n        \n        if (sIdx !== -1 && eIdx !== -1 && isSameDay(date, actualStart)) {\n          const startCol = sIdx * periods.length + 2;\n          const endCol = eIdx * periods.length + periods.length + 1;\n          return (\n            <div key={`holiday-range-${holiday.name}-${date.toISOString()}`}\n                 className=\"event-card holiday-card\"\n                 style={{ gridColumn: `${startCol} / ${endCol}`, gridRow: 3 }}>\n              {holiday.name}\n            </div>\n          );\n        }\n      }\n    }\n    \n    return null;\n  });\n\n  const scheduleEventItems = events.flatMap(e => {\n    const eStart = parseISO(e.startDate);\n    const eEnd = parseISO(e.endDate);\n    const viewStart = displayDates[0];\n    const viewEnd = displayDates[displayDates.length - 1];\n    \n    if (isAfter(eStart, viewEnd) || isBefore(eEnd, viewStart)) return [];\n\n    const startDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, eStart));\n    const endDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, eEnd));\n    const startPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === e.startPeriodId);\n    const endPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === e.endPeriodId);\n\n    if (startDayIdx === -1 || endDayIdx === -1) return [];\n\n    const startCol = startDayIdx * periods.length + startPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const endCol = endDayIdx * periods.length + endPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const span = endCol - startCol + 1;\n\n    // リソース固有の予定\n    if (e.resourceIds && e.resourceIds.length > 0) {\n      return e.resourceIds.map(resId => {\n        const resourceIdx = filteredResources.findIndex(r => r.id === resId);\n        if (resourceIdx === -1) return null;\n\n        return (\n          <div key={`event-${e.id}-${resId}`} \n               className=\"event-card schedule-event-card\"\n               style={{ \n                 gridColumn: `${startCol} / span ${span}`, \n                 gridRow: resourceIdx + 4,\n                 backgroundColor: e.color\n               }}>\n            {e.name}\n          </div>\n        );\n      }).filter(Boolean);\n    }\n\n    // 全体の予定\n    return [(\n      <div key={`event-${e.id}`} \n           className=\"event-card schedule-event-card\"\n           style={{ \n             gridColumn: `${startCol} / span ${span}`, \n             gridRow: 3,\n             backgroundColor: e.color\n           }}>\n        {e.name}\n      </div>\n    )];\n  });\n\n  const resourceLabels = filteredResources.map((r, idx) => (\n    <div key={`label-${r.id}`} className=\"grid-label\" style={{ gridColumn: 1, gridRow: idx + 4 }}>\n      {r.name}\n    </div>\n  ));\n\n  const lessonItems = lessons.flatMap(l => {\n    const lStart = parseISO(l.startDate);\n    const lEnd = parseISO(l.endDate);\n    const viewStart = displayDates[0];\n    const viewEnd = displayDates[displayDates.length - 1];\n\n    if (isAfter(lStart, viewEnd) || isBefore(lEnd, viewStart)) return [];\n    \n    const startDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, lStart));\n    const endDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, lEnd));\n    const startPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.startPeriodId);\n    const endPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.endPeriodId);\n\n    if (startDayIdx === -1 || endDayIdx === -1) return [];\n\n    const startCol = startDayIdx * periods.length + startPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const endCol = endDayIdx * periods.length + endPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const span = endCol - startCol + 1;\n\n    // 関連するリソースIDを特定\n    let targetResIds: string[] = [];\n    if (viewMode === 'room') targetResIds = [l.roomId];\n    else if (viewMode === 'teacher') targetResIds = [l.teacherId, ...(l.subTeacherIds || [])];\n    else if (viewMode === 'course') targetResIds = [l.courseId];\n\n    return targetResIds.map(resId => {\n      const resourceIdx = filteredResources.findIndex(r => r.id === resId);\n      if (resourceIdx === -1) return null;\n\n      const infoItems = [];\n      if (viewMode !== 'room') infoItems.push({ label: labels.room, value: getResourceName(l.roomId) });\n      if (viewMode !== 'teacher') {\n        const allTeachers = [l.teacherId, ...(l.subTeacherIds || [])].map(id => getResourceName(id)).join(', ');\n        infoItems.push({ label: labels.teacher, value: allTeachers });\n      }\n      if (viewMode !== 'course') infoItems.push({ label: labels.course, value: getResourceName(l.courseId) });\n      const tooltipText = `${l.subject}\\n` + infoItems.map(item => `${item.label}: ${item.value}`).join('\\n');\n\n      return (\n        <div \n          key={`lesson-${l.id}-${resId}`} \n          className=\"lesson-card\"\n          style={{\n            gridColumn: `${startCol} / span ${span}`,\n            gridRow: resourceIdx + 4\n          }}\n          title={tooltipText}\n        >\n          <div className=\"lesson-subject\">{l.subject}</div>\n          <div className=\"lesson-details\">\n            {infoItems.map((item, idx) => (\n              <div key={idx} className=\"lesson-info\">\n                {item.label}: {item.value}\n              </div>\n            ))}\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      );\n    }).filter(Boolean);\n  });\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"timetable-wrapper\">\n      <div className=\"timetable-container\" style={gridStyle}>\n        <div className=\"grid-corner\" style={{ gridColumn: 1, gridRow: \"1 / span 2\" }} />\n        {filteredResources.map((_, rIdx) => \n          displayDates.map((date, dIdx) => {\n            const isSun = date.getDay() === 0;\n            const isSat = date.getDay() === 6;\n            const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n            let cellClass = 'grid-cell';\n            if (isSun) cellClass += ' is-sunday';\n            if (isSat) cellClass += ' is-saturday';\n            if (holiday) cellClass += ' is-holiday';\n            return periods.map((_, pIdx) => (\n              <div key={`cell-${rIdx}-${dIdx}-${pIdx}`} \n                   className={cellClass} \n                   style={{ gridColumn: dIdx * periods.length + pIdx + 2, gridRow: rIdx + 4 }} />\n            ));\n          })\n        )}\n        {dateHeaders}\n        {periodHeaders}\n        {eventLabel}\n        {eventCells}\n        {holidayItems}\n        {scheduleEventItems}\n        {resourceLabels}\n        {lessonItems}\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n",
    "file_path": "src/components/Timetable.tsx"
  }
}

---

## MODEL ✨

I have successfully implemented the requested enhancements for the User, Teacher, and Lesson models.

**Key updates:**
- **User/Teacher Association**: Linked the `User` (with role `TEACHER`) to a corresponding `Resource` of type `teacher` in the database (`backend/prisma/schema.prisma`) and frontend types.
- **Multiple Sub-Teachers**: Updated the `Lesson` model to support one main teacher and multiple sub-teachers. The `Timetable` component now displays a lesson in the rows of both the main teacher and all assigned sub-teachers.
- **Resource-Specific Schedules**: Enhanced the `ScheduleEvent` model to allow linking events to specific resources (teachers, rooms, etc.). These events now appear directly in the resource's row in the timetable, while unlinked events remain in the top "event" row.
- **Documentation**: Updated `GEMINI.md` and `src/types.ts` to reflect the new data structures and functionality.

These changes provide greater flexibility in resource management and scheduling, allowing for complex team-teaching scenarios and individual resource planning.

---

## USER 🧑‍💻

- ScheduleEvent は、必要に応じ、イベント行に表示するかを制御できます。
- ScheduleEvent にリソースが割り当てられた場合には、該当するリソースの行にも表示します。
- Lesson に サブの講師が割り当てられた場合は、ラベルにサブ講師を表示するとともに該当するサブ講師の行にも Lesson を表示します。

## MODEL ✨

I will update the `ScheduleEvent` model in both `src/types.ts` and `backend/prisma/schema.prisma` to include a `showInEventRow` boolean flag. This will allow for granular control over whether an event appears in the main event row, in addition to its visibility in specific resource rows when assigned.

## MODEL ✨

I will now update `src/components/Timetable.tsx` to display `ScheduleEvent` items in the event row if `showInEventRow` is true (or if it's a global event without assigned resources). I'll also modify the `Lesson` card logic to include a "sub-teacher" line in the tooltip and card details, ensuring all teachers are clearly listed when viewing from any of their respective rows.
**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "write_file",
  "args": {
    "file_path": "src/components/Timetable.tsx",
    "content": "import { TimePeriod, Resource, Lesson, ResourceType, ViewType, Holiday, ResourceLabels, ScheduleEvent } from '../types';\nimport { format, addDays, isSameDay, parseISO, getYear, differenceInDays, isWithinInterval, isBefore, isAfter, startOfDay } from 'date-fns';\nimport './Timetable.css';\n\ninterface Props {\n  periods: TimePeriod[];\n  resources: Resource[];\n  lessons: Lesson[];\n  events: ScheduleEvent[];\n  viewMode: ResourceType;\n  viewType: ViewType;\n  baseDate: Date;\n  holidays: Holiday[];\n  labels: ResourceLabels;\n}\n\nexport function Timetable({ periods, resources, lessons, events, viewMode, viewType, baseDate, holidays, labels }: Props) {\n  const locale = navigator.language;\n  const dateFormatter = new Intl.DateTimeFormat(locale, { month: 'short', day: 'numeric', weekday: 'short' });\n\n  const getResourceName = (id: string) => {\n    return resources.find(r => r.id === id)?.name || id;\n  };\n\n  const getHoliday = (date: Date) => {\n    const target = startOfDay(date);\n    return holidays.find(h => {\n      if (h.date) return isSameDay(target, parseISO(h.date));\n      if (h.start && h.end) {\n        const start = startOfDay(parseISO(h.start));\n        const end = startOfDay(parseISO(h.end));\n        return (isSameDay(target, start) || isAfter(target, start)) && \n               (isSameDay(target, end) || isBefore(target, end));\n      }\n      return false;\n    });\n  };\n\n  const getDayCount = () => {\n    if (viewType === 'day') return 1;\n    if (viewType === 'week') return 7;\n    if (viewType === 'month') return 30;\n    if (viewType === 'year') {\n      const start = new Date(getYear(baseDate), 3, 1);\n      const end = new Date(getYear(baseDate) + 1, 2, 31);\n      return differenceInDays(end, start) + 1;\n    }\n    return 1;\n  };\n\n  const dayCount = getDayCount();\n  const displayDates = Array.from({ length: dayCount }).map((_, i) => addDays(baseDate, i));\n\n  const filteredResources = resources\n    .filter(r => r.type === viewMode)\n    .sort((a, b) => (a.order ?? 0) - (b.order ?? 0));\n\n  const colWidth = '60px';\n  const gridStyle = {\n    display: 'grid',\n    gridTemplateColumns: `150px repeat(${displayDates.length * periods.length}, minmax(${colWidth}, 1fr))`,\n    gridTemplateRows: `40px 30px 80px repeat(${filteredResources.length}, 80px)`,\n  };\n\n  const dateHeaders = displayDates.map((date, dIdx) => {\n    const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n    const isSun = date.getDay() === 0;\n    const isSat = date.getDay() === 6;\n    const isFirstOfMonth = date.getDate() === 1;\n\n    let className = 'date-header';\n    if (isSun) className += ' is-sunday';\n    if (isSat) className += ' is-saturday';\n    if (holiday) className += ' is-holiday';\n    if (isFirstOfMonth) className += ' month-start';\n\n    return (\n      <div key={`date-${date.toISOString()}`} \n           className={className} \n           style={{ gridColumn: `${dIdx * periods.length + 2} / span ${periods.length}`, gridRow: 1 }}\n           title={holiday?.name}\n      >\n        {dateFormatter.format(date)}\n      </div>\n    );\n  });\n\n  const periodHeaders = displayDates.flatMap((date, dIdx) => \n    periods.map((p, pIdx) => {\n      const isSun = date.getDay() === 0;\n      const isSat = date.getDay() === 6;\n      const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n      let className = 'period-header';\n      if (isSun) className += ' is-sunday';\n      if (isSat) className += ' is-saturday';\n      if (holiday) className += ' is-holiday';\n\n      return (\n        <div key={`period-${date.toISOString()}-${p.id}`} \n             className={className} \n             style={{ gridColumn: dIdx * periods.length + pIdx + 2, gridRow: 2 }}>\n          {p.name}\n        </div>\n      );\n    })\n  );\n\n  const eventLabel = (\n    <div key=\"label-event\" className=\"event-label\" style={{ gridColumn: 1, gridRow: 3 }}>\n      {labels.event}\n    </div>\n  );\n\n  const eventCells = displayDates.flatMap((date, dIdx) => {\n    const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n    const isSun = date.getDay() === 0;\n    const isSat = date.getDay() === 6;\n    let className = 'grid-cell event-cell';\n    if (isSun) className += ' is-sunday';\n    if (isSat) className += ' is-saturday';\n    if (holiday) className += ' is-holiday';\n\n    return periods.map((_, pIdx) => (\n      <div key={`event-cell-${dIdx}-${pIdx}`} \n           className={className} \n           style={{ gridColumn: dIdx * periods.length + pIdx + 2, gridRow: 3 }} />\n    ));\n  });\n\n  const holidayItems = displayDates.map((date, dIdx) => {\n    const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n    if (!holiday) return null;\n\n    if (holiday.date && isSameDay(date, parseISO(holiday.date))) {\n      return (\n        <div key={`holiday-${date.toISOString()}`}\n             className=\"event-card holiday-card\"\n             style={{ gridColumn: `${dIdx * periods.length + 2} / span ${periods.length}`, gridRow: 3 }}>\n          {holiday.name}\n        </div>\n      );\n    }\n    \n    const hStart = holiday.start ? parseISO(holiday.start) : null;\n    const hEnd = holiday.end ? parseISO(holiday.end) : null;\n    \n    if (hStart && hEnd) {\n      if (isSameDay(date, hStart) || (isSameDay(date, displayDates[0]) && isAfter(date, hStart) && isBefore(date, hEnd))) {\n        const actualStart = isAfter(hStart, displayDates[0]) ? hStart : displayDates[0];\n        const actualEnd = isBefore(hEnd, displayDates[displayDates.length - 1]) ? hEnd : displayDates[displayDates.length - 1];\n        \n        const sIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, actualStart));\n        const eIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, actualEnd));\n        \n        if (sIdx !== -1 && eIdx !== -1 && isSameDay(date, actualStart)) {\n          const startCol = sIdx * periods.length + 2;\n          const endCol = eIdx * periods.length + periods.length + 1;\n          return (\n            <div key={`holiday-range-${holiday.name}-${date.toISOString()}`}\n                 className=\"event-card holiday-card\"\n                 style={{ gridColumn: `${startCol} / ${endCol}`, gridRow: 3 }}>\n              {holiday.name}\n            </div>\n          );\n        }\n      }\n    }\n    \n    return null;\n  });\n\n  const scheduleEventItems = events.flatMap(e => {\n    const eStart = parseISO(e.startDate);\n    const eEnd = parseISO(e.endDate);\n    const viewStart = displayDates[0];\n    const viewEnd = displayDates[displayDates.length - 1];\n    \n    if (isAfter(eStart, viewEnd) || isBefore(eEnd, viewStart)) return [];\n\n    const startDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, eStart));\n    const endDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, eEnd));\n    const startPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === e.startPeriodId);\n    const endPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === e.endPeriodId);\n\n    if (startDayIdx === -1 || endDayIdx === -1) return [];\n\n    const startCol = startDayIdx * periods.length + startPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const endCol = endDayIdx * periods.length + endPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const span = endCol - startCol + 1;\n\n    const result = [];\n\n    // リソース固有の予定\n    if (e.resourceIds && e.resourceIds.length > 0) {\n      e.resourceIds.forEach(resId => {\n        const resourceIdx = filteredResources.findIndex(r => r.id === resId);\n        if (resourceIdx !== -1) {\n          result.push(\n            <div key={`event-${e.id}-${resId}`} \n                 className=\"event-card schedule-event-card\"\n                 style={{ \n                   gridColumn: `${startCol} / span ${span}`, \n                   gridRow: resourceIdx + 4,\n                   backgroundColor: e.color\n                 }}>\n              {e.name}\n            </div>\n          );\n        }\n      });\n    }\n\n    // イベント行（row 3）に表示する場合\n    // (showInEventRow が undefined または true、またはリソース指定がない場合)\n    if (e.showInEventRow !== false || !e.resourceIds || e.resourceIds.length === 0) {\n      result.push(\n        <div key={`event-${e.id}-global`} \n             className=\"event-card schedule-event-card\"\n             style={{ \n               gridColumn: `${startCol} / span ${span}`, \n               gridRow: 3,\n               backgroundColor: e.color\n             }}>\n          {e.name}\n        </div>\n      );\n    }\n\n    return result;\n  });\n\n  const resourceLabels = filteredResources.map((r, idx) => (\n    <div key={`label-${r.id}`} className=\"grid-label\" style={{ gridColumn: 1, gridRow: idx + 4 }}>\n      {r.name}\n    </div>\n  ));\n\n  const lessonItems = lessons.flatMap(l => {\n    const lStart = parseISO(l.startDate);\n    const lEnd = parseISO(l.endDate);\n    const viewStart = displayDates[0];\n    const viewEnd = displayDates[displayDates.length - 1];\n\n    if (isAfter(lStart, viewEnd) || isBefore(lEnd, viewStart)) return [];\n    \n    const startDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, lStart));\n    const endDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, lEnd));\n    const startPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.startPeriodId);\n    const endPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.endPeriodId);\n\n    if (startDayIdx === -1 || endDayIdx === -1) return [];\n\n    const startCol = startDayIdx * periods.length + startPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const endCol = endDayIdx * periods.length + endPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const span = endCol - startCol + 1;\n\n    // 関連するリソースIDを特定\n    let targetResIds: string[] = [];\n    if (viewMode === 'room') targetResIds = [l.roomId];\n    else if (viewMode === 'teacher') targetResIds = [l.teacherId, ...(l.subTeacherIds || [])];\n    else if (viewMode === 'course') targetResIds = [l.courseId];\n\n    return targetResIds.map(resId => {\n      const resourceIdx = filteredResources.findIndex(r => r.id === resId);\n      if (resourceIdx === -1) return null;\n\n      const infoItems = [];\n      if (viewMode !== 'room') infoItems.push({ label: labels.room, value: getResourceName(l.roomId) });\n      \n      // 講師表示 (メイン + サブ)\n      const mainTeacherName = getResourceName(l.teacherId);\n      const subTeacherNames = (l.subTeacherIds || []).map(id => getResourceName(id));\n      \n      if (viewMode !== 'teacher') {\n        const allTeachers = [mainTeacherName, ...subTeacherNames].join(', ');\n        infoItems.push({ label: labels.teacher, value: allTeachers });\n      } else {\n        // 講師別表示の場合、サブ講師がいれば明記する\n        if (subTeacherNames.length > 0) {\n          if (resId === l.teacherId) {\n            infoItems.push({ label: 'サブ', value: subTeacherNames.join(', ') });\n          } else {\n            infoItems.push({ label: 'メイン', value: mainTeacherName });\n            const otherSubTeachers = subTeacherNames.filter(name => name !== getResourceName(resId));\n            if (otherSubTeachers.length > 0) {\n              infoItems.push({ label: '他サブ', value: otherSubTeachers.join(', ') });\n            }\n          }\n        }\n      }\n\n      if (viewMode !== 'course') infoItems.push({ label: labels.course, value: getResourceName(l.courseId) });\n      const tooltipText = `${l.subject}\\n` + infoItems.map(item => `${item.label}: ${item.value}`).join('\\n');\n\n      return (\n        <div \n          key={`lesson-${l.id}-${resId}`} \n          className=\"lesson-card\"\n          style={{\n            gridColumn: `${startCol} / span ${span}`,\n            gridRow: resourceIdx + 4\n          }}\n          title={tooltipText}\n        >\n          <div className=\"lesson-subject\">{l.subject}</div>\n          <div className=\"lesson-details\">\n            {infoItems.map((item, idx) => (\n              <div key={idx} className=\"lesson-info\">\n                {item.label}: {item.value}\n              </div>\n            ))}\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      );\n    }).filter(Boolean);\n  });\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"timetable-wrapper\">\n      <div className=\"timetable-container\" style={gridStyle}>\n        <div className=\"grid-corner\" style={{ gridColumn: 1, gridRow: \"1 / span 2\" }} />\n        {filteredResources.map((_, rIdx) => \n          displayDates.map((date, dIdx) => {\n            const isSun = date.getDay() === 0;\n            const isSat = date.getDay() === 6;\n            const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n            let cellClass = 'grid-cell';\n            if (isSun) cellClass += ' is-sunday';\n            if (isSat) cellClass += ' is-saturday';\n            if (holiday) cellClass += ' is-holiday';\n            return periods.map((_, pIdx) => (\n              <div key={`cell-${rIdx}-${dIdx}-${pIdx}`} \n                   className={cellClass} \n                   style={{ gridColumn: dIdx * periods.length + pIdx + 2, gridRow: rIdx + 4 }} />\n            ));\n          })\n        )}\n        {dateHeaders}\n        {periodHeaders}\n        {eventLabel}\n        {eventCells}\n        {holidayItems}\n        {scheduleEventItems}\n        {resourceLabels}\n        {lessonItems}\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n"
  }
}

---

## MODEL ✨

I have refined the display logic for `ScheduleEvent` and `Lesson` to handle sub-teachers and resource-specific visibility more effectively.

**Key enhancements:**
- **ScheduleEvent Control**: Added a `showInEventRow` flag to `ScheduleEvent`. Events are now displayed in the top event row if this flag is true or if they are "global" (no resource assigned). If resources are assigned, the event also appears in each assigned resource's specific row.
- **Lesson Display for Sub-Teachers**: Lessons now appear in the rows of all assigned sub-teachers when in "teacher" view mode. The lesson card labels have been improved to clearly distinguish between the "main" teacher and "sub" teachers when viewing from their respective rows.
- **Enhanced Labels**: Updated the information displayed on `Lesson` cards to include sub-teacher names, providing better context at a glance.

These changes ensure that all schedule information is accurately represented across different views, making it easier for users to track overlapping responsibilities and resource-specific events.

  "id": "read_file_1774700757583_0",

getYear, getMonth, parseISO } from 'date-fns';\n\nconst BACKEND_URL = 'http://localhost:3001/api';\n\nexport function App() {\n  const viewMode = useSignal<ResourceType>('room');\n  const viewType = useSignal<ViewType>('day');\n  const currentDate = useSignal<Date>(new Date('2026-03-26'));\n  const holidays = useSignal<Holiday[]>([]);\n  const isHolidayMode = useSignal<boolean>(false);\n  const resources = useSignal<Resource[]>([]);\n  const lessons = useSignal<Lesson[]>([]);\n  const events = useSignal<ScheduleEvent[]>([]);\n\n  // Auth signals\n  const user = useSignal<User | null>(null);\n  const token = useSignal<string | null>(null);\n  const authError = useSignal<string | undefined>(undefined);\n\n  // リソースの表示名設定\n  const resourceLabels = useSignal<ResourceLabels>({\n    room: '教室',\n    teacher: '講師',\n    course: '講座',\n    event: 'イベント'\n  });\n\n  // 初期化時にlocalStorageからセッション復元\n  useEffect(() => {\n    const savedToken = localStorage.getItem('auth_token');\n    const savedUser = localStorage.getItem('auth_user');\n    if (savedToken && savedUser) {\n      token.value = savedToken;\n      user.value = JSON.parse(savedUser);\n    }\n  }, []);\n\n  const fetchData = async () => {\n    if (!token.value) return;\n\n    try {\n      const headers = {\n        'Authorization': `Bearer ${token.value}`\n      };\n      \n      const [resResources, resLessons, resEvents, resHolidays] = await Promise.all([\n        fetch(`${BACKEND_URL}/resources`, { headers }),\n        fetch(`${BACKEND_URL}/lessons`, { headers }),\n        fetch(`${BACKEND_URL}/events`, { headers }),\n        fetch(`${BACKEND_URL}/holidays`, { headers })\n      ]);\n\n      if (resResources.status === 401) {\n        handleLogout();\n        return;\n      }\n\n      resources.value = await resResources.json();\n      lessons.value = await resLessons.json();\n      events.value = await resEvents.json();\n      holidays.value = await resHolidays.json();\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Failed to fetch data from backend:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (token.value) {\n      fetchData();\n    }\n  }, [token.value]);\n\n  const handleLogin = async (email: string, pass: string) => {\n    authError.value = undefined;\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${BACKEND_URL}/auth/login`, {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        body: JSON.stringify({ email, password: pass })\n      });\n\n      const data: AuthResponse & { error?: string } = await res.json();\n\n      if (!res.ok) {\n        authError.value = data.error || 'Login failed';\n        return;\n      }\n\n      token.value = data.token;\n      user.value = data.user;\n      localStorage.setItem('auth_token', data.token);\n      localStorage.setItem('auth_user', JSON.stringify(data.user));\n    } catch (err) {\n      authError.value = 'Server connection failed';\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleLogout = () => {\n    token.value = null;\n    user.value = null;\n    localStorage.removeItem('auth_token');\n    localStorage.removeItem('auth_user');\n  };\n\n  if (!token.value) {\n    return <Login onLogin={handleLogin} error={authError.value} />;\n  }\n\n  const moveDate = (amount: number) => {\n    if (viewType.value === 'day') currentDate.value = addDays(currentDate.value, amount);\n    if (viewType.value === 'week') currentDate.value = addDays(currentDate.value, amount * 7);\n    if (viewType.value === 'month') currentDate.value = addDays(currentDate.value, amount * 30);\n    if (viewType.value === 'year') currentDate.value = addDays(currentDate.value, amount * 365);\n  };\n\n  const handleDateChange = (e: any) => {\n    const newDate = parseISO(e.target.value);\n    if (!isNaN(newDate.getTime())) {\n      currentDate.value = newDate;\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleViewTypeChange = (type: ViewType) => {\n    viewType.value = type;\n    if (type === 'year') {\n      const year = getMonth(currentDate.value) < 3 ? getYear(currentDate.value) - 1 : getYear(currentDate.value);\n      currentDate.value = new Date(year, 3, 1);\n    }\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"app-container\">\n      <header className=\"app-header\">\n        <div className=\"header-top\">\n          <h1>EduGrid Scheduler</h1>\n          {user.value && (\n            <div className=\"user-info\">\n              <span className=\"user-email\">{user.value.email} ({user.value.role})</span>\n              <button className=\"logout-button\" onClick={handleLogout}>Sign Out</button>\n            </div>\n          )}\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"controls\">\n          <div className=\"control-group\">\n            <button onClick={() => viewMode.value = 'room'}>{resourceLabels.value.room}</button>\n            <button onClick={() => viewMode.value = 'teacher'}>{resourceLabels.value.teacher}</button>\n            <button onClick={() => viewMode.value = 'course'}>{resourceLabels.value.course}</button>\n          </div>\n\n          <div className=\"control-group\">\n            <button onClick={() => handleViewTypeChange('day')}>1日</button>\n            <button onClick={() => handleViewTypeChange('week')}>1週間</button>\n            <button onClick={() => handleViewTypeChange('month')}>1ヶ月</button>\n            <button onClick={() => handleViewTypeChange('year')}>1年</button>\n          </div>\n\n          <div className=\"control-group date-nav\">\n            <button onClick={() => moveDate(-1)}>前へ</button>\n            <input \n              type=\"date\" \n              className=\"date-picker\"\n              value={format(currentDate.value, 'yyyy-MM-dd')}\n              onChange={handleDateChange}\n            />\n            <button onClick={() => moveDate(1)}>次へ</button>\n          </div>\n\n          <label className=\"holiday-toggle\">\n            <input \n              type=\"checkbox\" \n              checked={isHolidayMode.value} \n              onChange={(e) => isHolidayMode.value = e.currentTarget.checked} \n            />\n            祝日テーマ\n          </label>\n        </div>\n      </header>\n\n      <div className={`timetable-view ${isHolidayMode.value ? 'holiday-theme' : ''}`}>\n        <Timetable \n          periods={DEFAULT_PERIODS}\n          resources={resources.value}\n          lessons={lessons.value}\n          events={events.value}\n          viewMode={viewMode.value}\n          viewType={viewType.value}\n          baseDate={currentDate.value}\n          holidays={holidays.value}\n          labels={resourceLabels.value}\n        />\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n"
  }
}
```

時限ヘッダーの直後に、祝日、休暇、学校行事（入学式、清掃等）を統合して表示する固定行。\n  - 祝日データおよびカスタムイベントデータの双方に対応。\n- **マルチビュー対応:**\n  - **1日 / 1週間 / 1ヶ月 / 1年 (4月始まり)** の表示切り替え。\n  - すべてのビューで時限の幅（60px）を一定に保ち、一貫した情報量を維持。\n- **国際化 (i18n) & 曜日表示:**\n  - ヘッダー（日付・時限・イベント）およびサイドバー（リソースラベル列）を固定し、スクロール時の一覧性を確保。\n  - 水平スクロール中もリソースラベルが画面外に消えないよう列を完全に固定し、セルの重なりや位置ズレが発生しないように制御する。\n  - 垂直スクロール時もヘッダー部分が固定される。\n\n## データインターフェース (Data Structures)\n\n```typescript\nexport type ViewType = 'day' | 'week' | 'month' | 'year';\nexport type ResourceType = 'room' | 'teacher' | 'course';\nexport type UserRole = 'ADMIN' | 'TEACHER' | 'STUDENT';\n\n// ユーザー定義\ninterface User {\n  id: string;\n  email: string;\n  role: UserRole;\n}\n\n// リソース定義 (Resource テーブル)\ninterface Resource {\n  id: string;\n  name: string;\n  type: ResourceType;\n  order: number;\n  userId?: string; // 紐付けられたユーザーID (講師の場合)\n}\n\n// 授業データ (Lesson テーブル)\ninterface Lesson {\n  id: string;\n  subject: string;\n  teacherId: string;\n  subTeacherIds?: string[]; // サブ講師\n  roomId: string;\n  courseId: string;\n  startDate: string;\n  startPeriodId: string;\n  endDate: string;\n  endPeriodId: string;\n}\n\n// スケジュールイベント (ScheduleEvent テーブル)\ninterface ScheduleEvent {\n  id: string;\n  name: string;\n  startDate: string;\n  startPeriodId: string;\n  endDate: string;\n  endPeriodId: string;\n  color?: string;\n  resourceIds?: string[]; // 紐付け先リソース（講師、教室など）\n}\n```\n\n## 開発・プロトタイプの状況\n\n- [x] Vite + Preact + TypeScript のセットアップ\n- [x] CSS Grid によるマルチビュー（1日/1週/1月/1年）の実装\n- [x] Sticky ヘッダー/サイドバーの完全実装\n- [x] イベント行の実装と祝日・行事の統合表示\n- [x] Node.js (Express) + Prisma + PostgreSQL によるバックエンド構築\n- [x] JWT による認証機能とロールベースアクセス制御（RBAC）\n- [x] フロントエンドのログイン画面とセッション管理の実装\n- [x] データベースからの動的データ取得（API連携）への移行\n- [x] 初期データ投入用シードスクリプトの作成\n- [x] `concurrently` によるフロントエンド・バックエンドの一括起動環境\n- [ ] ドラッグ＆ドロップによる授業の移動・編集機能\n- [ ] AI によるスケジューリング最適化/支援機能の検討\n"

## MODEL ✨

The `e.showInEventRow !== false` logic accurately defaults to true when the flag is undefined or explicitly true. Furthermore, empty `e.resourceIds` correctly trigger global event display in the event row. I've finished the task.
I have implemented the requested features to enhance the `ScheduleEvent` and `Lesson` functionality.

### Key Changes:

- **Enhanced `ScheduleEvent` Visibility**:
    - Added a `showInEventRow` flag (defaulting to true) to `ScheduleEvent`.
    - Events assigned to specific resources will now appear in those resources' rows.
    - Global events (no resources assigned) or events with `showInEventRow: true` will continue to appear in the top event row.
- **Improved `Lesson` Sub-Teacher Support**:
    - Lessons now appear in the rows for both the main teacher and all assigned sub-teachers when in "teacher" view mode.
    - Updated lesson cards and tooltips to explicitly list the main and sub-teachers, using the labels defined in the settings.
- **Configurable Teacher Labels**:
    - Added `mainTeacher` and `subTeacher` to the `ResourceLabels` configuration.
    - Replaced hardcoded strings ("Main", "Sub") with these configurable labels throughout the `Timetable` component.
    - Default labels are set to "メイン" (Main) and "サブ" (Sub).
- **Documentation and Types**:
    - Updated `GEMINI.md`, `backend/prisma/schema.prisma`, and `src/types.ts` to reflect the updated data structures and new configuration options.

These improvements ensure that complex schedules with team-teaching or resource-specific events are clearly and accurately represented in the timetable.

## USER 🧑‍💻

- サブの講師は、同等に扱います。「他」などの prefix をつける必要がありません。
- 1ヶ月、1年のビューの時限の列幅は、1週間と同じ列幅にします。
- ここまでの仕様を Gemini.md に反映してください。
- 本日、新たに増えた仕様について、試験データを追加し、追加したデータを確認するための日付やビューを教えてください。

I have updated the specifications and mock data as requested.

### Updates:
- **Consistent Column Width**: Ensured all views (Day, Week, Month, Year) maintain a consistent 60px width for time slots to provide a uniform experience across different time scales.
- **Equal Treatment for Sub-Teachers**: Removed the "Other" prefix. Main and sub-teachers are now listed equally in labels.
- **GEMINI.md**: Updated with the latest specifications for display logic, column widths, and data structures.
- **Mock Data Enhancement**: Added new test cases in `src/types.ts` to verify sub-teacher and event visibility logic.

### How to Verify (Test Data):
**Date**: `2026-03-26` (The default date when starting the app)
**View Mode**: Change to `講師` (Teacher)

1.  **Multiple Sub-Teachers**:
    - Look at the row for **佐藤 先生 (t1)**. You will see "チームティーチング:総合探究" at 3-4 periods.
    - Check the rows for **鈴木 先生 (t2)** and **高橋 先生 (t3)**. The same lesson appears in their rows as well.
    - Hover or look at the details; all three teachers are listed using the configured `mainTeacher`/`subTeacher` labels without any "Other" prefix.
2.  **Resource-Only Events**:
    - Look at the row for **加藤 先生 (t10)**. You will see "出張（学会参加）" spanning the whole day (1-8 periods).
    - Note that this event **does not** appear in the top "イベント" (Event) row because `showInEventRow` is set to `false`.
3.  **Global-Only Events**:
    - Look at the top **イベント** (Event) row. You will see "全館避難訓練" at 5-6 periods.
    - This event **does not** appear in any specific resource row because no `resourceIds` are assigned.
4.  **Events in Both Rows**:
    - Look at the top **イベント** (Event) row and the row for **田中 先生 (t4)** (and **104号室** if in Room mode).
    - You will see "研究授業（公開）" at 2-3 periods in both the event row and the resource row.
5.  **Multi-View Width**:
    - Switch between `1日`, `1週間`, `1ヶ月`, and `1年`.
    - Observe that the horizontal scale (60px per slot) remains consistent, ensuring the same level of detail is available in all views.

### 更新内容:
- **講師とユーザーの紐付け**: 佐藤先生（t1）を `sato@example.com` ユーザーに紐付けました。
- **チームティーチング（サブ講師）**: 3月26日の「チームティーチング:総合探究」に佐藤先生、鈴木先生、高橋先生を割り当てました。
- **リソース固有の予定**: 
    - 加藤先生（t10）にのみ表示される「出張（学会参加）」を追加（イベント行には非表示）。
    - 田中先生（t4）と104号室（r4）の両方の行、およびイベント行に表示される「研究授業（公開）」を追加。
- **共通パスワード**: テストの便宜上、シードされる全ユーザーのパスワードを `password123` に統一しました。

### データの確認方法:
バックエンドのディレクトリでシードを実行してください（既に実行環境が整っている場合）:
```bash
cd backend
npx prisma db seed
```

その後、フロントエンドで以下の日付・ビューを確認してください：
- **日付**: `2026-03-26`
- **講師ビュー**:
    - **佐藤先生、鈴木先生、高橋先生**の行に「チームティーチング:総合探究」が表示されます。
    - **加藤先生**の行に「出張（学会参加）」が表示されます（イベント行には出ません）。
    - **田中先生**の行に「研究授業（公開）」が表示されます。
- **教室ビュー**:
    - **104号室**の行に「研究授業（公開）」が表示されます。
- **イベント行（最上部）**:
    - 「全館避難訓練」や「研究授業（公開）」が表示されますが、「出張」は表示されません。

## USER 🧑‍💻

- 3月26日の「チームティーチング:総合探究」が佐藤先生のみに表示されてしまいます。また、サブ講師等のラベルもありません。図形に収まらない場合は、ポップアップにのみ表示でも構いません。
- 「出張（学会参加）」が加藤先生（t10）の行に表示されず、イベント行に表示されてしまいます。
- 「研究授業（公開）」は、イベント行だけに表示されてしまいます。
- 3月26日がビューの開始日になっている場合、ほとんどの項目が表示できていません。
- イベント行に時間が重なるイベントがある場合は、高さを調整して、ずらして表示できると良い。

    "output": "import { TimePeriod, Resource, Lesson, ResourceType, ViewType, Holiday, ResourceLabels, ScheduleEvent } from '../types';\nimport { format, addDays, isSameDay, parseISO, getYear, differenceInDays, isWithinInterval, isBefore, isAfter, startOfDay } from 'date-fns';\nimport './Timetable.css';\n\ninterface Props {\n  periods: TimePeriod[];\n  resources: Resource[];\n  lessons: Lesson[];\n  events: ScheduleEvent[];\n  viewMode: ResourceType;\n  viewType: ViewType;\n  baseDate: Date;\n  holidays: Holiday[];\n  labels: ResourceLabels;\n}\n\nexport function Timetable({ periods, resources, lessons, events, viewMode, viewType, baseDate, holidays, labels }: Props) {\n  const locale = navigator.language;\n  const dateFormatter = new Intl.DateTimeFormat(locale, { month: 'short', day: 'numeric', weekday: 'short' });\n\n  const getResourceName = (id: string) => {\n    return resources.find(r => r.id === id)?.name || id;\n  };\n\n  const getHoliday = (date: Date) => {\n    const target = startOfDay(date);\n    return holidays.find(h => {\n      if (h.date) return isSameDay(target, parseISO(h.date));\n      if (h.start && h.end) {\n        const start = startOfDay(parseISO(h.start));\n        const end = startOfDay(parseISO(h.end));\n        return (isSameDay(target, start) || isAfter(target, start)) && \n               (isSameDay(target, end) || isBefore(target, end));\n      }\n      return false;\n    });\n  };\n\n  const getDayCount = () => {\n    if (viewType === 'day') return 1;\n    if (viewType === 'week') return 7;\n    if (viewType === 'month') return 30;\n    if (viewType === 'year') {\n      const start = new Date(getYear(baseDate), 3, 1);\n      const end = new Date(getYear(baseDate) + 1, 2, 31);\n      return differenceInDays(end, start) + 1;\n    }\n    return 1;\n  };\n\n  const dayCount = getDayCount();\n  const displayDates = Array.from({ length: dayCount }).map((_, i) => addDays(baseDate, i));\n\n  const filteredResources = resources\n    .filter(r => r.type === viewMode)\n    .sort((a, b) => (a.order ?? 0) - (b.order ?? 0));\n\n  const colWidth = '60px';\n  const gridStyle = {\n    display: 'grid',\n    gridTemplateColumns: `150px repeat(${displayDates.length * periods.length}, minmax(${colWidth}, 1fr))`,\n    gridTemplateRows: `40px 30px 80px repeat(${filteredResources.length}, 80px)`,\n  };\n\n  const dateHeaders = displayDates.map((date, dIdx) => {\n    const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n    const isSun = date.getDay() === 0;\n    const isSat = date.getDay() === 6;\n    const isFirstOfMonth = date.getDate() === 1;\n\n    let className = 'date-header';\n    if (isSun) className += ' is-sunday';\n    if (isSat) className += ' is-saturday';\n    if (holiday) className += ' is-holiday';\n    if (isFirstOfMonth) className += ' month-start';\n\n    return (\n      <div key={`date-${date.toISOString()}`} \n           className={className} \n           style={{ gridColumn: `${dIdx * periods.length + 2} / span ${periods.length}`, gridRow: 1 }}\n           title={holiday?.name}\n      >\n        {dateFormatter.format(date)}\n      </div>\n    );\n  });\n\n  const periodHeaders = displayDates.flatMap((date, dIdx) => \n    periods.map((p, pIdx) => {\n      const isSun = date.getDay() === 0;\n      const isSat = date.getDay() === 6;\n      const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n      let className = 'period-header';\n      if (isSun) className += ' is-sunday';\n      if (isSat) className += ' is-saturday';\n      if (holiday) className += ' is-holiday';\n\n      return (\n        <div key={`period-${date.toISOString()}-${p.id}`} \n             className={className} \n             style={{ gridColumn: dIdx * periods.length + pIdx + 2, gridRow: 2 }}>\n          {p.name}\n        </div>\n      );\n    })\n  );\n\n  const eventLabel = (\n    <div key=\"label-event\" className=\"event-label\" style={{ gridColumn: 1, gridRow: 3 }}>\n      {labels.event}\n    </div>\n  );\n\n  const eventCells = displayDates.flatMap((date, dIdx) => {\n    const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n    const isSun = date.getDay() === 0;\n    const isSat = date.getDay() === 6;\n    let className = 'grid-cell event-cell';\n    if (isSun) className += ' is-sunday';\n    if (isSat) className += ' is-saturday';\n    if (holiday) className += ' is-holiday';\n\n    return periods.map((_, pIdx) => (\n      <div key={`event-cell-${dIdx}-${pIdx}`} \n           className={className} \n           style={{ gridColumn: dIdx * periods.length + pIdx + 2, gridRow: 3 }} />\n    ));\n  });\n\n  const holidayItems = displayDates.map((date, dIdx) => {\n    const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n    if (!holiday) return null;\n\n    if (holiday.date && isSameDay(date, parseISO(holiday.date))) {\n      return (\n        <div key={`holiday-${date.toISOString()}`}\n             className=\"event-card holiday-card\"\n             style={{ gridColumn: `${dIdx * periods.length + 2} / span ${periods.length}`, gridRow: 3 }}>\n          {holiday.name}\n        </div>\n      );\n    }\n    \n    const hStart = holiday.start ? parseISO(holiday.start) : null;\n    const hEnd = holiday.end ? parseISO(holiday.end) : null;\n    \n    if (hStart && hEnd) {\n      if (isSameDay(date, hStart) || (isSameDay(date, displayDates[0]) && isAfter(date, hStart) && isBefore(date, hEnd))) {\n        const actualStart = isAfter(hStart, displayDates[0]) ? hStart : displayDates[0];\n        const actualEnd = isBefore(hEnd, displayDates[displayDates.length - 1]) ? hEnd : displayDates[displayDates.length - 1];\n        \n        const sIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, actualStart));\n        const eIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, actualEnd));\n        \n        if (sIdx !== -1 && eIdx !== -1 && isSameDay(date, actualStart)) {\n          const startCol = sIdx * periods.length + 2;\n          const endCol = eIdx * periods.length + periods.length + 1;\n          return (\n            <div key={`holiday-range-${holiday.name}-${date.toISOString()}`}\n                 className=\"event-card holiday-card\"\n                 style={{ gridColumn: `${startCol} / ${endCol}`, gridRow: 3 }}>\n              {holiday.name}\n            </div>\n          );\n        }\n      }\n    }\n    \n    return null;\n  });\n\n  const scheduleEventItems = events.flatMap(e => {\n    const eStart = parseISO(e.startDate);\n    const eEnd = parseISO(e.endDate);\n    const viewStart = displayDates[0];\n    const viewEnd = displayDates[displayDates.length - 1];\n    \n    if (isAfter(eStart, viewEnd) || isBefore(eEnd, viewStart)) return [];\n\n    const startDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, eStart));\n    const endDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, eEnd));\n    const startPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === e.startPeriodId);\n    const endPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === e.endPeriodId);\n\n    if (startDayIdx === -1 || endDayIdx === -1) return [];\n\n    const startCol = startDayIdx * periods.length + startPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const endCol = endDayIdx * periods.length + endPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const span = endCol - startCol + 1;\n\n    const result = [];\n\n    // リソース固有の予定\n    if (e.resourceIds && e.resourceIds.length > 0) {\n      e.resourceIds.forEach(resId => {\n        const resourceIdx = filteredResources.findIndex(r => r.id === resId);\n        if (resourceIdx !== -1) {\n          result.push(\n            <div key={`event-${e.id}-${resId}`} \n                 className=\"event-card schedule-event-card\"\n                 style={{ \n                   gridColumn: `${startCol} / span ${span}`, \n                   gridRow: resourceIdx + 4,\n                   backgroundColor: e.color\n                 }}>\n              {e.name}\n            </div>\n          );\n        }\n      });\n    }\n\n    // イベント行（row 3）に表示する場合\n    // (showInEventRow が undefined または true、またはリソース指定がない場合)\n    if (e.showInEventRow !== false || !e.resourceIds || e.resourceIds.length === 0) {\n      result.push(\n        <div key={`event-${e.id}-global`} \n             className=\"event-card schedule-event-card\"\n             style={{ \n               gridColumn: `${startCol} / span ${span}`, \n               gridRow: 3,\n               backgroundColor: e.color\n             }}>\n          {e.name}\n        </div>\n      );\n    }\n\n    return result;\n  });\n\n  const resourceLabels = filteredResources.map((r, idx) => (\n    <div key={`label-${r.id}`} className=\"grid-label\" style={{ gridColumn: 1, gridRow: idx + 4 }}>\n      {r.name}\n    </div>\n  ));\n\n  const lessonItems = lessons.flatMap(l => {\n    const lStart = parseISO(l.startDate);\n    const lEnd = parseISO(l.endDate);\n    const viewStart = displayDates[0];\n    const viewEnd = displayDates[displayDates.length - 1];\n\n    if (isAfter(lStart, viewEnd) || isBefore(lEnd, viewStart)) return [];\n    \n    const startDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, lStart));\n    const endDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, lEnd));\n    const startPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.startPeriodId);\n    const endPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.endPeriodId);\n\n    if (startDayIdx === -1 || endDayIdx === -1) return [];\n\n    const startCol = startDayIdx * periods.length + startPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const endCol = endDayIdx * periods.length + endPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const span = endCol - startCol + 1;\n\n    // 関連するリソースIDを特定\n    let targetResIds: string[] = [];\n    if (viewMode === 'room') targetResIds = [l.roomId];\n    else if (viewMode === 'teacher') targetResIds = [l.teacherId, ...(l.subTeacherIds || [])];\n    else if (viewMode === 'course') targetResIds = [l.courseId];\n\n    return targetResIds.map(resId => {\n      const resourceIdx = filteredResources.findIndex(r => r.id === resId);\n      if (resourceIdx === -1) return null;\n\n      const infoItems = [];\n      if (viewMode !== 'room') infoItems.push({ label: labels.room, value: getResourceName(l.roomId) });\n      \n      // 講師表示 (メイン + サブ)\n      const mainTeacherName = getResourceName(l.teacherId);\n      const subTeacherNames = (l.subTeacherIds || []).map(id => getResourceName(id));\n      \n      if (viewMode !== 'teacher') {\n        const allTeachers = [mainTeacherName, ...subTeacherNames].join(', ');\n        infoItems.push({ label: labels.teacher, value: allTeachers });\n      } else {\n        // 講師別表示の場合、サブ講師がいれば明記する\n        if (subTeacherNames.length > 0) {\n          if (resId === l.teacherId) {\n            infoItems.push({ label: labels.subTeacher, value: subTeacherNames.join(', ') });\n          } else {\n            infoItems.push({ label: labels.mainTeacher, value: mainTeacherName });\n            const otherSubTeachers = subTeacherNames.filter(id => getResourceName(id) !== getResourceName(resId));\n            if (otherSubTeachers.length > 0) {\n              infoItems.push({ label: labels.subTeacher, value: otherSubTeachers.join(', ') });\n            }\n          }\n        }\n      }\n\n      if (viewMode !== 'course') infoItems.push({ label: labels.course, value: getResourceName(l.courseId) });\n      const tooltipText = `${l.subject}\\n` + infoItems.map(item => `${item.label}: ${item.value}`).join('\\n');\n\n      return (\n        <div \n          key={`lesson-${l.id}-${resId}`} \n          className=\"lesson-card\"\n          style={{\n            gridColumn: `${startCol} / span ${span}`,\n            gridRow: resourceIdx + 4\n          }}\n          title={tooltipText}\n        >\n          <div className=\"lesson-subject\">{l.subject}</div>\n          <div className=\"lesson-details\">\n            {infoItems.map((item, idx) => (\n              <div key={idx} className=\"lesson-info\">\n                {item.label}: {item.value}\n              </div>\n            ))}\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      );\n    }).filter(Boolean);\n  });\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"timetable-wrapper\">\n      <div className=\"timetable-container\" style={gridStyle}>\n        <div className=\"grid-corner\" style={{ );\n}\n"
  }
