## MODEL ✨

I'll start by updating the `Lesson` and `ScheduleEvent` interfaces in `src/types.ts` to include the `subTeachers` and `resources` fields, each as an array of objects containing an `id` string. This change will ensure consistency with the backend data structure.
**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "replace",
  "args": {
    "file_path": "src/types.ts",
    "new_string": "export interface ScheduleEvent {\n  id: string;\n  name: string;\n  startDate: string;\n  startPeriodId: string;\n  endDate: string;\n  endPeriodId: string;\n  color?: string;\n  resourceIds?: string[]; // 紐付けられたリソースID（講師、教室など）\n  resources?: { id: string }[]; // バックエンドからのリレーション\n  showInEventRow?: boolean; // イベント行（最上部）に表示するかどうか\n}\n\nexport interface Lesson {\n  id: string;\n  subject: string;\n  teacherId: string;\n  subTeacherIds?: string[]; // サブ講師\n  subTeachers?: { id: string }[]; // バックエンドからのリレーション\n  roomId: string;\n  courseId: string;\n  startDate: string;   // 開始日 \"2026-03-26\"\n  startPeriodId: string; // 開始時限 \"p1\"\n  endDate: string;     // 終了日 \"2026-03-27\"\n  endPeriodId: string;   // 終了時限 \"p4\"\n}",
    "instruction": "Update Lesson and ScheduleEvent types to match backend relation structure.",
    "old_string": "export interface ScheduleEvent {\n  id: string;\n  name: string;\n  startDate: string;\n  startPeriodId: string;\n  endDate: string;\n  endPeriodId: string;\n  color?: string;\n  resourceIds?: string[]; // 紐付けられたリソースID（講師、教室など）\n  showInEventRow?: boolean; // イベント行（最上部）に表示するかどうか\n}\n\nexport interface Lesson {\n  id: string;\n  subject: string;\n  teacherId: string;\n  subTeacherIds?: string[]; // サブ講師\n  roomId: string;\n  courseId: string;\n  startDate: string;   // 開始日 \"2026-03-26\"\n  startPeriodId: string; // 開始時限 \"p1\"\n  endDate: string;     // 終了日 \"2026-03-27\"\n  endPeriodId: string;   // 終了時限 \"p4\"\n}"
```

## MODEL ✨

I'll fix `Timetable.tsx` by implementing `startOfDay` for consistent date comparisons and updating the logic to correctly handle both `resourceIds` and `resources`. I'll also add an overlap-detection mechanism for events in row 3 to calculate the proper `top` offset and ensure teacher labels are displayed correctly, even in sub-teacher rows.
**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "write_file",
  "args": {
    "file_path": "src/components/Timetable.tsx",
    "content": "import { TimePeriod, Resource, Lesson, ResourceType, ViewType, Holiday, ResourceLabels, ScheduleEvent } from '../types';\nimport { format, addDays, isSameDay, parseISO, getYear, differenceInDays, isWithinInterval, isBefore, isAfter, startOfDay } from 'date-fns';\nimport './Timetable.css';\n\ninterface Props {\n  periods: TimePeriod[];\n  resources: Resource[];\n  lessons: Lesson[];\n  events: ScheduleEvent[];\n  viewMode: ResourceType;\n  viewType: ViewType;\n  baseDate: Date;\n  holidays: Holiday[];\n  labels: ResourceLabels;\n}\n\nexport function Timetable({ periods, resources, lessons, events, viewMode, viewType, baseDate, holidays, labels }: Props) {\n  const locale = navigator.language;\n  const dateFormatter = new Intl.DateTimeFormat(locale, { month: 'short', day: 'numeric', weekday: 'short' });\n\n  const getResourceName = (id: string) => {\n    return resources.find(r => r.id === id)?.name || id;\n  };\n\n  const currentViewStart = startOfDay(baseDate);\n\n  const getHoliday = (date: Date) => {\n    const target = startOfDay(date);\n    return holidays.find(h => {\n      if (h.date) return isSameDay(target, startOfDay(parseISO(h.date)));\n      if (h.start && h.end) {\n        const start = startOfDay(parseISO(h.start));\n        const end = startOfDay(parseISO(h.end));\n        return (isSameDay(target, start) || isAfter(target, start)) && \n               (isSameDay(target, end) || isBefore(target, end));\n      }\n      return false;\n    });\n  };\n\n  const getDayCount = () => {\n    if (viewType === 'day') return 1;\n    if (viewType === 'week') return 7;\n    if (viewType === 'month') return 30;\n    if (viewType === 'year') {\n      const start = new Date(getYear(baseDate), 3, 1);\n      const end = new Date(getYear(baseDate) + 1, 2, 31);\n      return differenceInDays(end, start) + 1;\n    }\n    return 1;\n  };\n\n  const dayCount = getDayCount();\n  const displayDates = Array.from({ length: dayCount }).map((_, i) => addDays(currentViewStart, i));\n  const currentViewEnd = startOfDay(displayDates[displayDates.length - 1]);\n\n  const filteredResources = resources\n    .filter(r => r.type === viewMode)\n    .sort((a, b) => (a.order ?? 0) - (b.order ?? 0));\n\n  const colWidth = '60px';\n  const gridStyle = {\n    display: 'grid',\n    gridTemplateColumns: `150px repeat(${displayDates.length * periods.length}, minmax(${colWidth}, 1fr))`,\n    gridTemplateRows: `40px 30px 80px repeat(${filteredResources.length}, 80px)`,\n  };\n\n  const dateHeaders = displayDates.map((date, dIdx) => {\n    const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n    const isSun = date.getDay() === 0;\n    const isSat = date.getDay() === 6;\n    const isFirstOfMonth = date.getDate() === 1;\n\n    let className = 'date-header';\n    if (isSun) className += ' is-sunday';\n    if (isSat) className += ' is-saturday';\n    if (holiday) className += ' is-holiday';\n    if (isFirstOfMonth) className += ' month-start';\n\n    return (\n      <div key={`date-${date.toISOString()}`} \n           className={className} \n           style={{ gridColumn: `${dIdx * periods.length + 2} / span ${periods.length}`, gridRow: 1 }}\n           title={holiday?.name}\n      >\n        {dateFormatter.format(date)}\n      </div>\n    );\n  });\n\n  const periodHeaders = displayDates.flatMap((date, dIdx) => \n    periods.map((p, pIdx) => {\n      const isSun = date.getDay() === 0;\n      const isSat = date.getDay() === 6;\n      const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n      let className = 'period-header';\n      if (isSun) className += ' is-sunday';\n      if (isSat) className += ' is-saturday';\n      if (holiday) className += ' is-holiday';\n\n      return (\n        <div key={`period-${date.toISOString()}-${p.id}`} \n             className={className} \n             style={{ gridColumn: dIdx * periods.length + pIdx + 2, gridRow: 2 }}>\n          {p.name}\n        </div>\n      );\n    })\n  );\n\n  const eventLabel = (\n    <div key=\"label-event\" className=\"event-label\" style={{ gridColumn: 1, gridRow: 3 }}>\n      {labels.event}\n    </div>\n  );\n\n  const eventCells = displayDates.flatMap((date, dIdx) => {\n    const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n    const isSun = date.getDay() === 0;\n    const isSat = date.getDay() === 6;\n    let className = 'grid-cell event-cell';\n    if (isSun) className += ' is-sunday';\n    if (isSat) className += ' is-saturday';\n    if (holiday) className += ' is-holiday';\n\n    return periods.map((_, pIdx) => (\n      <div key={`event-cell-${dIdx}-${pIdx}`} \n           className={className} \n           style={{ gridColumn: dIdx * periods.length + pIdx + 2, gridRow: 3 }} />\n    ));\n  });\n\n  // イベント行（row 3）に表示する全アイテムの競合チェック\n  type Placement = { id: string; start: number; end: number; level: number; element: JSX.Element };\n  const row3Placements: Placement[] = [];\n\n  const getPlacementLevel = (start: number, end: number) => {\n    let level = 0;\n    while (true) {\n      const conflict = row3Placements.some(p => p.level === level && !(end < p.start || start > p.end));\n      if (!conflict) return level;\n      level++;\n    }\n  };\n\n  const holidayItems = displayDates.flatMap((date, dIdx) => {\n    const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n    if (!holiday) return [];\n\n    if (holiday.date && isSameDay(date, startOfDay(parseISO(holiday.date)))) {\n      const startCol = dIdx * periods.length + 2;\n      const endCol = dIdx * periods.length + periods.length + 1;\n      const level = getPlacementLevel(startCol, endCol - 1);\n      const el = (\n        <div key={`holiday-${date.toISOString()}`}\n             className=\"event-card holiday-card\"\n             style={{ \n               gridColumn: `${startCol} / ${endCol}`, \n               gridRow: 3,\n               top: `${72 + level * 22}px`\n             }}>\n          {holiday.name}\n        </div>\n      );\n      row3Placements.push({ id: `holiday-${date.toISOString()}`, start: startCol, end: endCol - 1, level, element: el });\n      return [el];\n    }\n    \n    const hStart = holiday.start ? startOfDay(parseISO(holiday.start)) : null;\n    const hEnd = holiday.end ? startOfDay(parseISO(holiday.end)) : null;\n    \n    if (hStart && hEnd) {\n      if (isSameDay(date, hStart) || (isSameDay(date, displayDates[0]) && isAfter(date, hStart) && isBefore(date, hEnd))) {\n        const actualStart = isAfter(hStart, displayDates[0]) ? hStart : displayDates[0];\n        const actualEnd = isBefore(hEnd, displayDates[displayDates.length - 1]) ? hEnd : displayDates[displayDates.length - 1];\n        \n        const sIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, actualStart));\n        const eIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, actualEnd));\n        \n        if (sIdx !== -1 && eIdx !== -1 && isSameDay(date, actualStart)) {\n          const startCol = sIdx * periods.length + 2;\n          const endCol = eIdx * periods.length + periods.length + 1;\n          const level = getPlacementLevel(startCol, endCol - 1);\n          const el = (\n            <div key={`holiday-range-${holiday.name}-${date.toISOString()}`}\n                 className=\"event-card holiday-card\"\n                 style={{ \n                   gridColumn: `${startCol} / ${endCol}`, \n                   gridRow: 3,\n                   top: `${72 + level * 22}px`\n                 }}>\n              {holiday.name}\n            </div>\n          );\n          row3Placements.push({ id: `holiday-range-${holiday.name}`, start: startCol, end: endCol - 1, level, element: el });\n          return [el];\n        }\n      }\n    }\n    \n    return [];\n  });\n\n  const scheduleEventItems = events.flatMap(e => {\n    const eStart = startOfDay(parseISO(e.startDate));\n    const eEnd = startOfDay(parseISO(e.endDate));\n    \n    if (isAfter(eStart, currentViewEnd) || isBefore(eEnd, currentViewStart)) return [];\n\n    const startDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, eStart));\n    const endDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, eEnd));\n    const startPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === e.startPeriodId);\n    const endPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === e.endPeriodId);\n\n    // ビュー外でも一部が掛かっている場合の調整\n    const sCol = (startDayIdx === -1) ? 2 : startDayIdx * periods.length + startPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const eCol = (endDayIdx === -1) ? (displayDates.length * periods.length + 1) : endDayIdx * periods.length + endPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const span = eCol - sCol + 1;\n\n    const result = [];\n    \n    // リソースIDのリストを統合\n    const resourceIdList = [\n      ...(e.resourceIds || []),\n      ...(e.resources || []).map(r => r.id)\n    ];\n\n    // リソース固有の予定\n    if (resourceIdList.length > 0) {\n      resourceIdList.forEach(resId => {\n        const resourceIdx = filteredResources.findIndex(r => r.id === resId);\n        if (resourceIdx !== -1) {\n          result.push(\n            <div key={`event-${e.id}-${resId}`} \n                 className=\"event-card schedule-event-card\"\n                 style={{ \n                   gridColumn: `${sCol} / span ${span}`, \n                   gridRow: resourceIdx + 4,\n                   backgroundColor: e.color\n                 }}>\n              {e.name}\n            </div>\n          );\n        }\n      });\n    }\n\n    // イベント行（row 3）に表示する場合\n    if (e.showInEventRow !== false || resourceIdList.length === 0) {\n      const level = getPlacementLevel(sCol, sCol + span - 1);\n      const el = (\n        <div key={`event-${e.id}-global`} \n             className=\"event-card schedule-event-card\"\n             style={{ \n               gridColumn: `${sCol} / span ${span}`, \n               gridRow: 3,\n               backgroundColor: e.color,\n               top: `${72 + level * 22}px`\n             }}>\n          {e.name}\n        </div>\n      );\n      row3Placements.push({ id: `event-${e.id}`, start: sCol, end: sCol + span - 1, level, element: el });\n      result.push(el);\n    }\n\n    return result;\n  });\n\n  const resourceLabels = filteredResources.map((r, idx) => (\n    <div key={`label-${r.id}`} className=\"grid-label\" style={{ gridColumn: 1, gridRow: idx + 4 }}>\n      {r.name}\n    </div>\n  ));\n\n  const lessonItems = lessons.flatMap(l => {\n    const lStart = startOfDay(parseISO(l.startDate));\n    const lEnd = startOfDay(parseISO(l.endDate));\n\n    if (isAfter(lStart, currentViewEnd) || isBefore(lEnd, currentViewStart)) return [];\n    \n    const startDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, lStart));\n    const endDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, lEnd));\n    const startPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.startPeriodId);\n    const endPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.endPeriodId);\n\n    const sCol = (startDayIdx === -1) ? 2 : startDayIdx * periods.length + startPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const eCol = (endDayIdx === -1) ? (displayDates.length * periods.length + 1) : endDayIdx * periods.length + endPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const span = eCol - sCol + 1;\n\n    const subIds = [\n      ...(l.subTeacherIds || []),\n      ...(l.subTeachers || []).map(t => t.id)\n    ];\n\n    // 関連するリソースIDを特定\n    let targetResIds: string[] = [];\n    if (viewMode === 'room') targetResIds = [l.roomId];\n    else if (viewMode === 'teacher') targetResIds = [l.teacherId, ...subIds];\n    else if (viewMode === 'course') targetResIds = [l.courseId];\n\n    return targetResIds.map(resId => {\n      const resourceIdx = filteredResources.findIndex(r => r.id === resId);\n      if (resourceIdx === -1) return null;\n\n      const infoItems = [];\n      if (viewMode !== 'room') infoItems.push({ label: labels.room, value: getResourceName(l.roomId) });\n      \n      const mainTeacherName = getResourceName(l.teacherId);\n      const subTeacherNames = subIds.map(id => getResourceName(id));\n      \n      if (viewMode !== 'teacher') {\n        const allTeachers = [mainTeacherName, ...subTeacherNames].join(', ');\n        infoItems.push({ label: labels.teacher, value: allTeachers });\n      } else {\n        if (subTeacherNames.length > 0) {\n          // メイン・サブ講師を分けずに表示（同等に扱う）\n          const allTeachers = [mainTeacherName, ...subTeacherNames].join(', ');\n          infoItems.push({ label: labels.teacher, value: allTeachers });\n        }\n      }\n\n      if (viewMode !== 'course') infoItems.push({ label: labels.course, value: getResourceName(l.courseId) });\n      const tooltipText = `${l.subject}\\n` + infoItems.map(item => `${item.label}: ${item.value}`).join('\\n');\n\n      return (\n        <div \n          key={`lesson-${l.id}-${resId}`} \n          className=\"lesson-card\"\n          style={{\n            gridColumn: `${sCol} / span ${span}`,\n            gridRow: resourceIdx + 4\n          }}\n          title={tooltipText}\n        >\n          <div className=\"lesson-subject\">{l.subject}</div>\n          <div className=\"lesson-details\">\n            {infoItems.map((item, idx) => (\n              <div key={idx} className=\"lesson-info\">\n                {item.label}: {item.value}\n              </div>\n            ))}\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      );\n    }).filter(Boolean);\n  });\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"timetable-wrapper\">\n      <div className=\"timetable-container\" style={gridStyle}>\n        <div className=\"grid-corner\" style={{ gridColumn: 1, gridRow: \"1 / span 2\" }} />\n        {filteredResources.map((_, rIdx) => \n          displayDates.map((date, dIdx) => {\n            const isSun = date.getDay() === 0;\n            const isSat = date.getDay() === 6;\n            const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n            let cellClass = 'grid-cell';\n            if (isSun) cellClass += ' is-sunday';\n            if (isSat) cellClass += ' is-saturday';\n            if (holiday) cellClass += ' is-holiday';\n            return periods.map((_, pIdx) => (\n              <div key={`cell-${rIdx}-${dIdx}-${pIdx}`} \n                   className={cellClass} \n                   style={{ gridColumn: dIdx * periods.length + pIdx + 2, gridRow: rIdx + 4 }} />\n            ));\n          })\n        )}\n        {dateHeaders}\n        {periodHeaders}\n        {eventLabel}\n        {eventCells}\n        {/* レベル別の配置を確保 */}\n        {holidayItems}\n        {scheduleEventItems}\n        {resourceLabels}\n        {lessonItems}\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n"
  }
}
```

2 : startDayIdx * periods.length + startPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const eCol = (endDayIdx === -1) ? (displayDates.length * periods.length + 1) : endDayIdx * periods.length + endPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const span = eCol - sCol + 1;\n\n    const result = [];\n    \n    // リソースIDのリストを統合\n    const resourceIdList = [\n      ...(e.resourceIds || []),\n      ...(e.resources || []).map(r => r.id)\n    ];\n\n    // リソース固有の予定\n    if (resourceIdList.length > 0) {\n      resourceIdList.forEach(resId => {\n        const resourceIdx = filteredResources.findIndex(r => r.id === resId);\n        if (resourceIdx !== -1) {\n          result.push(\n            <div key={`event-${e.id}-${resId}`} \n                 className=\"event-card schedule-event-card\"\n                 style={{ \n                   gridColumn: `${sCol} / span ${span}`, \n                   gridRow: resourceIdx + 4,\n                   backgroundColor: e.color\n                 }}>\n              {e.name}\n            </div>\n...\n        }\n      });\n    }\n\n    // イベント行（row 3）に表示する場合\n    if (e.showInEventRow !== false || resourceIdList.length === 0) {\n      const level = getPlacementLevel(sCol, sCol + span - 1);\n      const el = (\n        <div key={`event-${e.id}-global`} \n             className=\"event-card schedule-event-card\"\n             style={{ \n               gridColumn: `${sCol} / span ${span}`, \n               gridRow: 3,\n               backgroundColor: e.color,\n               top: `${72 + level * 22}px`\n             }}>\n          {e.name}\n        </div>\n      );\n      row3Placements.push({ id: `event-${e.id}`, start: sCol, end: sCol + span - 1, level, element: el });\n      result.push(el);\n    }\n\n    return result;\n  });\n\n...\n      {r.name}\n    </div>\n  ));\n\n  const lessonItems = lessons.flatMap(l => {\n    const lStart = startOfDay(parseISO(l.startDate));\n    const lEnd = startOfDay(parseISO(l.endDate));\n\n    if (isAfter(lStart, currentViewEnd) || isBefore(lEnd, currentViewStart)) return [];\n    \n    const startDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, lStart));\n    const endDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, lEnd));\n    const startPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.startPeriodId);\n    const endPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.endPeriodId);\n\n    const sCol = (startDayIdx === -1) ? 2 : startDayIdx * periods.length + startPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const eCol = (endDayIdx === -1) ? (displayDates.length * periods.length + 1) : endDayIdx * periods.length + endPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const span = eCol - sCol + 1;\n\n    const subIds = [\n      ...(l.subTeacherIds || []),\n      ...(l.subTeachers || []).map(t => t.id)\n    ];\n\n    // 関連するリソースIDを特定\n    let targetResIds: string[] = [];\n    if (viewMode === 'room') targetResIds = [l.roomId];\n    else if (viewMode === 'teacher') targetResIds = [l.teacherId, ...subIds];\n    else if (viewMode === 'course') targetResIds = [l.courseId];\n\n    return targetResIds.map(resId => {\n      const resourceIdx = filteredResources.findIndex(r => r.id === resId);\n      if (resourceIdx === -1) return null;\n\n      const infoItems = [];\n      if (viewMode !== 'room') infoItems.push({ label: labels.room, value: getResourceName(l.roomId) });\n      \n      const mainTeacherName = getResourceName(l.teacherId);\n      const subTeacherNames = subIds.map(id => getResourceName(id));\n      \n      if (viewMode !== 'teacher') {\n        const allTeachers = [mainTeacherName, ...subTeacherNames].join(', ');\n        infoItems.push({ label: labels.teacher, value: allTeachers });\n      } else {\n        if (subTeacherNames.length > 0) {\n          // メイン・サブ講師を分けずに表示（同等に扱う）\n          const allTeachers = [mainTeacherName, ...subTeacherNames].join(', ');\n          infoItems.push({ label: labels.teacher, value: allTeachers });\n        }\n      }\n\n      if (viewMode !== 'course') infoItems.push({ label: labels.course, value: getResourceName(l.courseId) });\n      const tooltipText = `${l.subject}\\n` + infoItems.map(item => `${item.label}: ${item.value}`).join('\\n');\n...\n      return (\n        <div \n          key={`lesson-${l.id}-${resId}`} \n          className=\"lesson-card\"\n          style={{\n            gridColumn: `${sCol} / span ${span}`,\n            gridRow: resourceIdx + 4\n          }}\n          title={tooltipText}\n        >\n          <div className=\"lesson-subject\">{l.subject}</div>\n...\n        )}\n        {dateHeaders}\n        {periodHeaders}\n        {eventLabel}\n        {eventCells}\n        {/* レベル別の配置を確保 */}\n        {holidayItems}\n        {scheduleEventItems}\n        {resourceLabels}\n        {lessonItems}\n      </div>\n..."
```json
  }
}
```

---

## MODEL ✨

不具合を修正し、仕様に合わせて表示ロジックを改善しました。

### 修正・改善内容：

1.  **開始日の表示不備の修正**:
    - 全ての日付比較において `startOfDay()` を適用するように統一しました。これにより、ビューの開始日（3月26日など）に予定されているイベントや授業が、時間帯のズレ（00:00:00 vs 09:00:00など）によってフィルタリングされてしまう問題を解消しました。
2.  **リレーションデータの処理改善**:
    - バックエンドから返される `subTeachers` や `resources`（オブジェクト配列）と、モックデータの `subTeacherIds` や `resourceIds`（ID配列）の両方を正しく処理できるようにロジックを強化しました。これにより、バックエンド連携時もサブ講師やリソース固有の予定が正しく表示されるようになりました。
3.  **チームティーチング（サブ講師）の表示**:
    - 授業に関連する全ての講師（メイン＋サブ）を特定し、それぞれの講師の行に同じ授業を表示するようにしました。
    - ラベルについても、サブ講師がいる場合は講師全員を並べて表示するように変更しました。
4.  **イベント行（3行目）の重なり制御**:
    - イベント行に表示される祝日、行事、全体の予定が時間的に重なる場合、垂直方向にレベルをずらして表示する（`top` オフセットを計算する）ロジックを実装しました。
5.  **イベントの表示場所の厳密な制御**:
    - `showInEventRow` フラグが `false` かつリソースが指定されている場合（例：「出張」）は、イベント行には表示せず、リソースの行にのみ表示するようにロジックを修正しました。
    - 「研究授業」のように両方に表示する設定も正しく機能します。

### 確認方法：
シードスクリプトを実行後、ブラウザで **2026-03-26** を確認してください。

- **講師ビュー**:
    - **佐藤、鈴木、高橋先生**のそれぞれの行に「チームティーチング:総合探究」が表示されます。
    - **加藤先生(t10)**の行に「出張」が表示されます（イベント行には表示されません）。
    - **田中先生(t4)**の行に「研究授業」が表示されます。
- **イベント行**:
    - 複数のイベント（避難訓練、研究授業、校内清掃など）が重なっている場合、上下にずれて表示されます。
    - 各項目の詳細はホバー時のツールチップ（またはブラウザのポップアップ）で確認できます。

## MODEL ✨

I have successfully implemented all requested enhancements, including data model updates, display logic fixes, and documentation improvements. I've updated `GEMINI.md` to reflect the current architectural state and added a comprehensive external deployment guide to `Deploy.md`. Finally, I've staged all changes, performed a detailed git commit, and pushed the updates to the remote repository.

### Summary of Changes:

- **Enhanced Display Logic**:
    - **Date Comparison**: Unified use of `startOfDay()` for all date comparisons to ensure consistent event visibility across all views.
    - **Event Row Overlap**: Implemented automatic vertical offsetting for overlapping events in the event row (row 3) to prevent visual clashes.
    - **Main/Sub-Teacher Treatment**: Main and sub-teachers are now treated equally, with labels showing all assigned teachers in both their respective rows and tooltips.
    - **Resource-Specific Events**: Corrected `showInEventRow` logic to accurately control event visibility in the global event row versus resource-specific rows.
- **Data Model & Backend Updates**:
    - **Prisma & Types**: Updated schema and shared types to support sub-teacher relations and resource-linked events.
    - **API Endpoints**: Modified `lessons` and `events` endpoints to include necessary relation data (`subTeachers`, `resources`).
    - **Seed Script**: Enhanced `backend/prisma/seed.ts` with comprehensive test data for sub-teachers and complex event visibility scenarios.
- **Documentation**:
    - **GEMINI.md**: Updated with the latest specifications for display behavior and data structures.
    - **Deploy.md**: Added a new section, "8. 外部アドレスでの公開 (External Deployment)," providing detailed steps for production setup, including environment variables, CORS, and Nginx configurations.
- **Git Operations**: Staged all modified files, performed a detailed commit, and successfully pushed to the remote `main` branch.

All changes are now live in the repository and ready for testing or deployment.

## MODEL ✨

I'll move the dynamic `colWidth` from inline styles to CSS variables in `src/components/Timetable.tsx`. This change will ensure more reliable and reactive width updates, addressing the issue where the 50px/60px adjustment wasn't always applied. I'll also modify the `gridStyle` to use these CSS variables.
**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "write_file",
  "args": {
    "file_path": "src/components/Timetable.tsx",
    "content": "import { TimePeriod, Resource, Lesson, ResourceType, ViewType, Holiday, ResourceLabels, ScheduleEvent } from '../types';\nimport { format, addDays, isSameDay, parseISO, getYear, differenceInDays, isWithinInterval, isBefore, isAfter, startOfDay } from 'date-fns';\nimport './Timetable.css';\n\ninterface Props {\n  periods: TimePeriod[];\n  resources: Resource[];\n  lessons: Lesson[];\n  events: ScheduleEvent[];\n  viewMode: ResourceType;\n  viewType: ViewType;\n  baseDate: Date;\n  holidays: Holiday[];\n  labels: ResourceLabels;\n}\n\nexport function Timetable({ periods, resources, lessons, events, viewMode, viewType, baseDate, holidays, labels }: Props) {\n  const locale = navigator.language;\n  const dateFormatter = new Intl.DateTimeFormat(locale, { month: 'short', day: 'numeric', weekday: 'short' });\n\n  const getResourceName = (id: string) => {\n    return resources.find(r => r.id === id)?.name || id;\n  };\n\n  const currentViewStart = startOfDay(baseDate);\n\n  const getHoliday = (date: Date) => {\n    const target = startOfDay(date);\n    return holidays.find(h => {\n      if (h.date) return isSameDay(target, startOfDay(parseISO(h.date)));\n      if (h.start && h.end) {\n        const start = startOfDay(parseISO(h.start));\n        const end = startOfDay(parseISO(h.end));\n        return (isSameDay(target, start) || isAfter(target, start)) && \n               (isSameDay(target, end) || isBefore(target, end));\n      }\n      return false;\n    });\n  };\n\n  const getDayCount = () => {\n    if (viewType === 'day') return 1;\n    if (viewType === 'week') return 7;\n    if (viewType === 'month') return 30;\n    if (viewType === 'year') {\n      const start = new Date(getYear(baseDate), 3, 1);\n      const end = new Date(getYear(baseDate) + 1, 2, 31);\n      return differenceInDays(end, start) + 1;\n    }\n    return 1;\n  };\n\n  const dayCount = getDayCount();\n  const displayDates = Array.from({ length: dayCount }).map((_, i) => addDays(currentViewStart, i));\n  const currentViewEnd = startOfDay(displayDates[displayDates.length - 1]);\n\n  const filteredResources = resources\n    .filter(r => r.type === viewMode)\n    .sort((a, b) => (a.order ?? 0) - (b.order ?? 0));\n\n  const colWidth = viewType === 'day' ? '60px' : '50px';\n  const gridStyle = {\n    '--col-width': colWidth,\n    display: 'grid',\n    gridTemplateColumns: `150px repeat(${displayDates.length * periods.length}, minmax(var(--col-width), 1fr))`,\n    gridTemplateRows: `40px 30px 80px repeat(${filteredResources.length}, 80px)`,\n  } as React.CSSProperties;\n\n  const dateHeaders = displayDates.map((date, dIdx) => {\n    const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n    const isSun = date.getDay() === 0;\n    const isSat = date.getDay() === 6;\n    const isFirstOfMonth = date.getDate() === 1;\n\n    let className = 'date-header';\n    if (isSun) className += ' is-sunday';\n    if (isSat) className += ' is-saturday';\n    if (holiday) className += ' is-holiday';\n    if (isFirstOfMonth) className += ' month-start';\n\n    return (\n      <div key={`date-${date.toISOString()}`} \n           className={className} \n           style={{ gridColumn: `${dIdx * periods.length + 2} / span ${periods.length}`, gridRow: 1 }}\n           title={holiday?.name}\n      >\n        {dateFormatter.format(date)}\n      </div>\n    );\n  });\n\n  const periodHeaders = displayDates.flatMap((date, dIdx) => \n    periods.map((p, pIdx) => {\n      const isSun = date.getDay() === 0;\n      const isSat = date.getDay() === 6;\n      const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n      let className = 'period-header';\n      if (isSun) className += ' is-sunday';\n      if (isSat) className += ' is-saturday';\n      if (holiday) className += ' is-holiday';\n\n      return (\n        <div key={`period-${date.toISOString()}-${p.id}`} \n             className={className} \n             style={{ gridColumn: dIdx * periods.length + pIdx + 2, gridRow: 2 }}>\n          {p.name}\n        </div>\n      );\n    })\n  );\n\n  const eventLabel = (\n    <div key=\"label-event\" className=\"event-label\" style={{ gridColumn: 1, gridRow: 3 }}>\n      {labels.event}\n    </div>\n  );\n\n  const eventCells = displayDates.flatMap((date, dIdx) => {\n    const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n    const isSun = date.getDay() === 0;\n    const isSat = date.getDay() === 6;\n    let className = 'grid-cell event-cell';\n    if (isSun) className += ' is-sunday';\n    if (isSat) className += ' is-saturday';\n    if (holiday) className += ' is-holiday';\n\n    return periods.map((_, pIdx) => (\n      <div key={`event-cell-${dIdx}-${pIdx}`} \n           className={className} \n           style={{ gridColumn: dIdx * periods.length + pIdx + 2, gridRow: 3 }} />\n    ));\n  });\n\n  // イベント行（row 3）に表示する全アイテムの競合チェック\n  type Placement = { id: string; start: number; end: number; level: number; element: JSX.Element };\n  const row3Placements: Placement[] = [];\n\n  const getPlacementLevel = (start: number, end: number) => {\n    let level = 0;\n    while (true) {\n      const conflict = row3Placements.some(p => p.level === level && !(end < p.start || start > p.end));\n      if (!conflict) return level;\n      level++;\n    }\n  };\n\n  const holidayItems = displayDates.flatMap((date, dIdx) => {\n    const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n    if (!holiday) return [];\n\n    if (holiday.date && isSameDay(date, startOfDay(parseISO(holiday.date)))) {\n      const startCol = dIdx * periods.length + 2;\n      const endCol = dIdx * periods.length + periods.length + 1;\n      const level = getPlacementLevel(startCol, endCol - 1);\n      const el = (\n        <div key={`holiday-${date.toISOString()}`}\n             className=\"event-card holiday-card\"\n             style={{ \n               gridColumn: `${startCol} / ${endCol}`, \n               gridRow: 3,\n               top: `${72 + level * 22}px`\n             }}>\n          {holiday.name}\n        </div>\n      );\n      row3Placements.push({ id: `holiday-${date.toISOString()}`, start: startCol, end: endCol - 1, level, element: el });\n      return [el];\n    }\n    \n    const hStart = holiday.start ? startOfDay(parseISO(holiday.start)) : null;\n    const hEnd = holiday.end ? startOfDay(parseISO(holiday.end)) : null;\n    \n    if (hStart && hEnd) {\n      if (isSameDay(date, hStart) || (isSameDay(date, displayDates[0]) && isAfter(date, hStart) && isBefore(date, hEnd))) {\n        const actualStart = isAfter(hStart, displayDates[0]) ? hStart : displayDates[0];\n        const actualEnd = isBefore(hEnd, displayDates[displayDates.length - 1]) ? hEnd : displayDates[displayDates.length - 1];\n        \n        const sIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, actualStart));\n        const eIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, actualEnd));\n        \n        if (sIdx !== -1 && eIdx !== -1 && isSameDay(date, actualStart)) {\n          const startCol = sIdx * periods.length + 2;\n          const endCol = eIdx * periods.length + periods.length + 1;\n          const level = getPlacementLevel(startCol, endCol - 1);\n          const el = (\n            <div key={`holiday-range-${holiday.name}-${date.toISOString()}`}\n                 className=\"event-card holiday-card\"\n                 style={{ \n                   gridColumn: `${startCol} / ${endCol}`, \n                   gridRow: 3,\n                   top: `${72 + level * 22}px`\n                 }}>\n              {holiday.name}\n            </div>\n          );\n          row3Placements.push({ id: `holiday-range-${holiday.name}`, start: startCol, end: endCol - 1, level, element: el });\n          return [el];\n        }\n      }\n    }\n    \n    return [];\n  });\n\n  const scheduleEventItems = events.flatMap(e => {\n    const eStart = startOfDay(parseISO(e.startDate));\n    const eEnd = startOfDay(parseISO(e.endDate));\n    \n    if (isAfter(eStart, currentViewEnd) || isBefore(eEnd, currentViewStart)) return [];\n\n    const startDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, eStart));\n    const endDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, eEnd));\n    const startPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === e.startPeriodId);\n    const endPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === e.endPeriodId);\n\n    // ビュー外でも一部が掛かっている場合の調整\n    const sCol = (startDayIdx === -1) ? 2 : startDayIdx * periods.length + startPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const eCol = (endDayIdx === -1) ? (displayDates.length * periods.length + 1) : endDayIdx * periods.length + endPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const span = eCol - sCol + 1;\n\n    const result = [];\n    \n    // リソースIDのリストを統合\n    const resourceIdList = [\n      ...(e.resourceIds || []),\n      ...(e.resources || []).map(r => r.id)\n    ];\n\n    // リソース固有の予定\n    if (resourceIdList.length > 0) {\n      resourceIdList.forEach(resId => {\n        const resourceIdx = filteredResources.findIndex(r => r.id === resId);\n        if (resourceIdx !== -1) {\n          result.push(\n            <div key={`event-${e.id}-${resId}`} \n                 className=\"event-card schedule-event-card\"\n                 style={{ \n                   gridColumn: `${sCol} / span ${span}`, \n                   gridRow: resourceIdx + 4,\n                   backgroundColor: e.color\n                 }}>\n              {e.name}\n            </div>\n          );\n        }\n      });\n    }\n\n    // イベント行（row 3）に表示する場合\n    if (e.showInEventRow !== false || resourceIdList.length === 0) {\n      const level = getPlacementLevel(sCol, sCol + span - 1);\n      const el = (\n        <div key={`event-${e.id}-global`} \n             className=\"event-card schedule-event-card\"\n             style={{ \n               gridColumn: `${sCol} / span ${span}`, \n               gridRow: 3,\n               backgroundColor: e.color,\n               top: `${72 + level * 22}px`\n             }}>\n          {e.name}\n        </div>\n      );\n      row3Placements.push({ id: `event-${e.id}`, start: sCol, end: sCol + span - 1, level, element: el });\n      result.push(el);\n    }\n\n    return result;\n  });\n\n  const resourceLabels = filteredResources.map((r, idx) => (\n    <div key={`label-${r.id}`} className=\"grid-label\" style={{ gridColumn: 1, gridRow: idx + 4 }}>\n      {r.name}\n    </div>\n  ));\n\n  const lessonItems = lessons.flatMap(l => {\n    const lStart = startOfDay(parseISO(l.startDate));\n    const lEnd = startOfDay(parseISO(l.endDate));\n\n    if (isAfter(lStart, currentViewEnd) || isBefore(lEnd, currentViewStart)) return [];\n    \n    const startDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, lStart));\n    const endDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, lEnd));\n    const startPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.startPeriodId);\n    const endPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.endPeriodId);\n\n    const sCol = (startDayIdx === -1) ? 2 : startDayIdx * periods.length + startPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const eCol = (endDayIdx === -1) ? (displayDates.length * periods.length + 1) : endDayIdx * periods.length + endPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const span = eCol - sCol + 1;\n\n    const subIds = [\n      ...(l.subTeacherIds || []),\n      ...(l.subTeachers || []).map(t => t.id)\n    ];\n\n    // 関連するリソースIDを特定\n    let targetResIds: string[] = [];\n    if (viewMode === 'room') targetResIds = [l.roomId];\n    else if (viewMode === 'teacher') targetResIds = [l.teacherId, ...subIds];\n    else if (viewMode === 'course') targetResIds = [l.courseId];\n\n    return targetResIds.map(resId => {\n      const resourceIdx = filteredResources.findIndex(r => r.id === resId);\n      if (resourceIdx === -1) return null;\n\n      const infoItems = [];\n      if (viewMode !== 'room') infoItems.push({ label: labels.room, value: getResourceName(l.roomId) });\n      \n      const mainTeacherName = getResourceName(l.teacherId);\n      const subTeacherNames = subIds.map(id => getResourceName(id));\n      \n      if (viewMode !== 'teacher') {\n        const allTeachers = [mainTeacherName, ...subTeacherNames].join(', ');\n        infoItems.push({ label: labels.teacher, value: allTeachers });\n      } else {\n        if (subTeacherNames.length > 0) {\n          // メイン・サブ講師を分けずに表示（同等に扱う）\n          const allTeachers = [mainTeacherName, ...subTeacherNames].join(', ');\n          infoItems.push({ label: labels.teacher, value: allTeachers });\n        }\n      }\n\n      if (viewMode !== 'course') infoItems.push({ label: labels.course, value: getResourceName(l.courseId) });\n      const tooltipText = `${l.subject}\\n` + infoItems.map(item => `${item.label}: ${item.value}`).join('\\n');\n\n      return (\n        <div \n          key={`lesson-${l.id}-${resId}`} \n          className=\"lesson-card\"\n          style={{\n            gridColumn: `${sCol} / span ${span}`,\n            gridRow: resourceIdx + 4\n          }}\n          title={tooltipText}\n        >\n          <div className=\"lesson-subject\">{l.subject}</div>\n          <div className=\"lesson-details\">\n            {infoItems.map((item, idx) => (\n              <div key={idx} className=\"lesson-info\">\n                {item.label}: {item.value}\n              </div>\n            ))}\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      );\n    }).filter(Boolean);\n  });\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"timetable-wrapper\">\n      <div className=\"timetable-container\" style={gridStyle}>\n        <div className=\"grid-corner\" style={{ gridColumn: 1, gridRow: \"1 / span 2\" }} />\n        {filteredResources.map((_, rIdx) => \n          displayDates.map((date, dIdx) => {\n            const isSun = date.getDay() === 0;\n            const isSat = date.getDay() === 6;\n            const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n            let cellClass = 'grid-cell';\n            if (isSun) cellClass += ' is-sunday';\n            if (isSat) cellClass += ' is-saturday';\n            if (holiday) cellClass += ' is-holiday';\n            return periods.map((_, pIdx) => (\n              <div key={`cell-${rIdx}-${dIdx}-${pIdx}`} \n                   className={cellClass} \n                   style={{ gridColumn: dIdx * periods.length + pIdx + 2, gridRow: rIdx + 4 }} />\n            ));\n          })\n        )}\n        {dateHeaders}\n        {periodHeaders}\n        {eventLabel}\n        {eventCells}\n        {/* レベル別の配置を確保 */}\n        {holidayItems}\n        {scheduleEventItems}\n        {resourceLabels}\n        {lessonItems}\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n"
  }
}
```

while (true) {\n      const conflict = row3Placements.some(p => p.level === level && !(end < p.start || start > p.end));\n      if (!conflict) return level;\n      level++;\n    }\n  };\n\n  const row3Placements.push({ id: `holiday-${date.toISOString()}`, start: startCol, end: endCol - 1, level, element: el });\n      return [el];\n    }\n    \n    const hStart = holiday.start ? startOfDay(parseISO(holiday.start)) : null;\n    const hEnd = holiday.end ? startOfDay(parseISO(holiday.end)) : null;\n    \n    if (hStart && hEnd) {\n      if (isSameDay(date, hStart) || (isSameDay(date, displayDates[0]) && isAfter(date, hStart) && isBefore(date, hEnd))) {\n        const actualStart = isAfter(hStart, displayDates[0]) ? hStart : displayDates[0];\n        const actualEnd = isBefore(hEnd, displayDates[displayDates.length - 1]) ? hEnd : displayDates[displayDates.length - 1];\n        \n        const sIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, actualStart));\n        const eIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, actualEnd));\n        \n        if (sIdx !== -1 && eIdx !== -1 && isSameDay(date, actualStart)) {\n          const startCol = sIdx * periods.length + 2;\n          const endCol = eIdx * periods.length + periods.length + 1;\n          const level = getPlacementLevel(startCol, endCol - 1);\n          const el = (\n            <div key={`holiday-range-${holiday.name}-${date.toISOString()}`}\n                 className=\"event-card holiday-card\"\n                 style={{ \n                   gridColumn: `${startCol} / ${endCol}`, \n                   gridRow: 3,\n                   top: `${72 + level * 22}px`\n                 }}>\n              {holiday.name}\n            </div>\n          );\n          row3Placements.push({ id: `holiday-range-${holiday.name}`, start: startCol, end: endCol - 1, level, element: el });\n          return [el];\n        }\n      }\n    }\n    \n    return [];\n  });\n\n  const scheduleEventItems = events.flatMap(e => {\n    const eStart = startOfDay(parseISO(e.startDate));\n    const eEnd = startOfDay(parseISO(e.endDate));\n    \n    if (isAfter(eStart, currentViewEnd) || isBefore(eEnd, currentViewStart)) return [];\n\n    const startDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, eStart));\n    const endDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, eEnd));\n    const startPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === e.startPeriodId);\n    const endPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === e.endPeriodId);\n\n    // ビュー外でも一部が掛かっている場合の調整\n    const sCol = (startDayIdx === -1) ? 2 : startDayIdx * periods.length + startPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const eCol = (endDayIdx === -1) ? (displayDates.length * periods.length + 1) : endDayIdx * periods.length + endPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const span = eCol - sCol + 1;\n\n    const result = [];\n    \n    // リソースIDのリストを統合\n    const resourceIdList = [\n      ...(e.resourceIds || []),\n      ...(e.resources || []).map(r => r.id)\n    ];\n\n    // リソース固有の予定\n    if (resourceIdList.length > 0) {\n      resourceIdList.forEach(resId => {\n        const resourceIdx = filteredResources.findIndex(r => r.id === resId);\n        if (resourceIdx !== -1) {\n          result.push(\n            <div key={`event-${e.id}-${resId}`} \n                 className=\"event-card schedule-event-card\"\n                 style={{ \n                   gridColumn: `${sCol} / span ${span}`, \n                   gridRow: resourceIdx + 4,\n                   backgroundColor: e.color\n                 }}>\n              {e.name}\n            </div>\n          );\n        }\n      });\n    }\n\n    // イベント行（row 3）に表示する場合\n    if (e.showInEventRow !== false || resourceIdList.length === 0) {\n      const level = getPlacementLevel(sCol, sCol + span - 1);\n      const el = (\n        <div key={`event-${e.id}-global`} \n             className=\"event-card schedule-event-card\"\n             style={{ \n               gridColumn: `${sCol} / span ${span}`, \n               gridRow: 3,\n               backgroundColor: e.color,\n               top: `${72 + level * 22}px`\n             }}>\n          {e.name}\n        </div>\n      );\n      row3Placements.push({ id: `event-${e.id}`, start: sCol, end: sCol + span - 1, level, element: el });\n      result.push(el);\n    }\n\n    return result;\n  });\n\n  const resourceLabels = filteredResources.map((r, idx) => (\n    <div key={`label-${r.id}`} className=\"grid-label\" style={{ gridColumn: 1, gridRow: idx + 4 }}>\n      {r.name}\n    </div>\n  ));\n\n  const lessonItems = lessons.flatMap(l => {\n    const lStart = startOfDay(parseISO(l.startDate));\n    const lEnd = startOfDay(parseISO(l.endDate));\n\n    if (isAfter(lStart, currentViewEnd) || isBefore(lEnd, currentViewStart)) return [];\n    \n    const startDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, lStart));\n    const endDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, lEnd));\n    const startPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.startPeriodId);\n    const endPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.endPeriodId);\n\n    const sCol = (startDayIdx === -1) ? 2 : startDayIdx * periods.length + startPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const eCol = (endDayIdx === -1) ? (displayDates.length * periods.length + 1) : endDayIdx * periods.length + endPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const span = eCol - sCol + 1;\n\n    const subIds = [\n      ...(l.subTeacherIds || []),\n      ...(l.subTeachers || []).map(t => t.id)\n    ];\n\n    // 関連するリソースIDを特定\n    let targetResIds: string[] = [];\n    if (viewMode === 'room') targetResIds = [l.roomId];\n    else if (viewMode === 'teacher') targetResIds = [l.teacherId, ...subIds];\n    else if (viewMode === 'course') targetResIds = [l.courseId];\n\n    return targetResIds.map(resId => {\n      const resourceIdx = filteredResources.findIndex(r => r.id === resId);\n      if (resourceIdx === -1) return null;\n\n      const infoItems = [];\n      if (viewMode !== 'room') infoItems.push({ label: labels.room, value: getResourceName(l.roomId) });\n      \n      const mainTeacherName = getResourceName(l.teacherId);\n      const subTeacherNames = subIds.map(id => getResourceName(id));\n      \n      if (viewMode !== 'teacher') {\n        const allTeachers = [mainTeacherName, ...subTeacherNames].join(', ');\n        infoItems.push({ label: labels.teacher, value: allTeachers });\n      } else {\n        if (subTeacherNames.length > 0) {\n          // メイン・サブ講師を分けずに表示（同等に扱う）\n          const allTeachers = [mainTeacherName, ...subTeacherNames].join(', ');\n          infoItems.push({ label: labels.teacher, value: allTeachers });\n        }\n      }\n\n      if (viewMode !== 'course') infoItems.push({ label: labels.course, value: getResourceName(l.courseId) });\n      const tooltipText = `${l.subject}\\n` + infoItems.map(item => `${item.label}: ${item.value}`).join('\\n');\n\n      return (\n        <div \n          key={`lesson-${l.id}-${resId}`} \n className=\"lesson-info\">\n                {item.label}: {item.value}\n              </div>\n            ))}\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      );\n    }).filter(Boolean);\n  });\n\n  return ("
```json
  }
}
```

## MODEL ✨

I've fixed the column width application issue when switching dates or views by making `gridTemplateColumns` more explicit and adding a unique `key` to the `timetable-container`. This forces the browser to recalculate the grid layout whenever relevant props change. I've also pushed the fix to the `main` branch.

開始日時の変更時にも列幅が正しく適用されるよう、以下の修正を行いました：

1.  **グリッド列の定義を厳格化**: `minmax` を使用せず、直接 `50px` または `60px` を指定するように変更しました。
2.  **コンテナに動的な `key` を追加**: `viewType`, `baseDate`, `viewMode`, `filteredResources.length` を組み合わせた `key` をグリッドコンテナに設定しました。これにより、日付やビューが変更された際に React がコンテナを完全に再生成（Re-mount）し、ブラウザによるグリッドレイアウトの再計算を強制するようにしました。

修正内容は Git に commit および push 済みです。

---

## USER 🧑‍💻

1日→1週間→1ヶ月→1年の順に切り替えると幅が適用されない。1年→1ヶ月→1週間の順に切り替えると1ヶ月と1週間には幅が適用されるが、1年に幅が適用されることがない。開始日時を変更した場合も幅が適用されない。という状態に戻りました。

---

## MODEL ✨

ブラウザのグリッド計算の限界や、要素の最大幅（特に年間ビューのような非常に広大なレイアウト）における制限、および React のレンダリングとブラウザのレイアウト更新のタイミングの問題が重なっている可能性があります。

より堅牢に、かつ強制的にレイアウトを再計算させるため、以下の修正を行います：

1.  **コンテナの幅をピクセル単位で明示的に計算**: `max-content` に頼らず、JavaScript で計算した合計ピクセル幅を `width` プロパティに直接設定します。
2.  **`grid-template-columns` の簡素化**: `repeat(N, width)` 形式を維持しつつ、コンテナ自体の幅を固定することでブラウザの計算負荷を軽減します。
3.  **CSS の `min-width` 指定を削除**: インラインスタイルの `width` と競合しないようにします。

### 1. `src/components/Timetable.tsx` の修正

一貫した計算と強制的な再描画のため、幅の計算を強化します。

## MODEL ✨

I have successfully addressed the grid layout issues by calculating the total pixel width in `src/components/Timetable.tsx` and applying it directly to the container's `width` style. I've also implemented a more robust `key` and removed the `min-width: max-content` from the CSS to ensure consistent and accurate rendering across all views and dates. These changes have been committed and pushed to the `main` branch.

ブラウザが巨大なグリッドのレイアウトを自動計算する際の不備を回避するため、以下の根本的な修正を行いました：

1.  **合計幅の完全な明示化**: `max-content` による自動計算に頼らず、JavaScript側で `150px + (列数 * 列幅)` を計算し、インラインスタイルの `width` にピクセル単位で直接指定するようにしました。
2.  **CSS の競合排除**: `Timetable.css` から `min-width: max-content` を削除し、JavaScript で計算された固定幅が常に優先されるようにしました。
3.  **再レンダリングの強制強化**: `key` に合計列数 (`totalCols`) を含めることで、ビューの切り替えや日付の変更によって列数が変わった際、React が確実にコンテナを再生成し、ブラウザが新しい幅でゼロからレイアウトを構成するようにしました。

修正内容は Git に commit および push 済みです。

## USER 🧑‍💻

幅の問題は解消しましたが、リソースラベルを表示する列がスクロールアウトする状態に戻ってしまいました。

---

## MODEL ✨

グリッドの合計幅を固定したことでレイアウトは安定しましたが、`width` の固定方法や `key` による再生成のタイミングにより、ブラウザが `position: sticky` のコンテキストを正しく認識できなくなった可能性があります。

特に、`display: grid` のコンテナ自体に `width` を指定すると、ブラウザによってはその内部の要素の `sticky` 判定がグリッドエリア内に制限されてしまうことがあります。

これを解決するため、以下の修正を行います：
1.  **コンテナの幅指定を `min-width` に変更**: `width` を固定するのではなく、`min-width` を使用して内容量に応じた幅を確保しつつ、`width: 100%` とすることで `sticky` の可動範囲を維持します。
2.  **`position: sticky` をインラインスタイルでも明示**: CSS クラスだけでなく、JS 側でも重要なプロパティを指定して確実に適用させます。
3.  **`Timetable.css` の調整**: 以前有効だった設定（`min-width: max-content` 等）を、固定幅計算と矛盾しない形で再調整します。

### 1. `src/components/Timetable.tsx` の修正

## MODEL ✨

全体を一括で `write_file` することで、微細な文字列の不一致によるエラーを回避し、確実に修正を適用します。

**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "write_file",
  "args": {
    "content": "import { TimePeriod, Resource, Lesson, ResourceType, ViewType, Holiday, ResourceLabels, ScheduleEvent } from '../types';\nimport { format, addDays, isSameDay, parseISO, getYear, differenceInDays, isWithinInterval, isBefore, isAfter, startOfDay } from 'date-fns';\nimport './Timetable.css';\n\ninterface Props {\n  periods: TimePeriod[];\n  resources: Resource[];\n  lessons: Lesson[];\n  events: ScheduleEvent[];\n  viewMode: ResourceType;\n  viewType: ViewType;\n  baseDate: Date;\n  holidays: Holiday[];\n  labels: ResourceLabels;\n}\n\nexport function Timetable({ periods, resources, lessons, events, viewMode, viewType, baseDate, holidays, labels }: Props) {\n  const locale = navigator.language;\n  const dateFormatter = new Intl.DateTimeFormat(locale, { month: 'short', day: 'numeric', weekday: 'short' });\n\n  const getResourceName = (id: string) => {\n    return resources.find(r => r.id === id)?.name || id;\n  };\n\n  const currentViewStart = startOfDay(baseDate);\n\n  const getHoliday = (date: Date) => {\n    const target = startOfDay(date);\n    return holidays.find(h => {\n      if (h.date) return isSameDay(target, startOfDay(parseISO(h.date)));\n      if (h.start && h.end) {\n        const start = startOfDay(parseISO(h.start));\n        const end = startOfDay(parseISO(h.end));\n        return (isSameDay(target, start) || isAfter(target, start)) && \n               (isSameDay(target, end) || isBefore(target, end));\n      }\n      return false;\n    });\n  };\n\n  const getDayCount = () => {\n    if (viewType === 'day') return 1;\n    if (viewType === 'week') return 7;\n    if (viewType === 'month') return 30;\n    if (viewType === 'year') {\n      const start = new Date(getYear(baseDate), 3, 1);\n      const end = new Date(getYear(baseDate) + 1, 2, 31);\n      return differenceInDays(end, start) + 1;\n    }\n    return 1;\n  };\n\n  const dayCount = getDayCount();\n  const displayDates = Array.from({ length: dayCount }).map((_, i) => addDays(currentViewStart, i));\n  const currentViewEnd = startOfDay(displayDates[displayDates.length - 1]);\n\n  const filteredResources = resources\n    .filter(r => r.type === viewMode)\n    .sort((a, b) => (a.order ?? 0) - (b.order ?? 0));\n\n  const colWidthNum = viewType === 'day' ? 60 : 50;\n  const colWidth = `${colWidthNum}px`;\n  const totalCols = displayDates.length * periods.length;\n  const totalWidth = 150 + totalCols * colWidthNum;\n\n  const gridStyle = {\n    '--col-width': colWidth,\n    display: 'grid',\n    width: '100%',\n    minWidth: `${totalWidth}px`,\n    gridTemplateColumns: `150px repeat(${totalCols}, ${colWidth})`,\n    gridTemplateRows: `40px 30px 80px repeat(${filteredResources.length || 0}, 80px)`,\n  } as React.CSSProperties;\n\n  const stickyLeft = { position: 'sticky', left: 0, zIndex: 25 } as React.CSSProperties;\n\n  const dateHeaders = displayDates.map((date, dIdx) => {\n    const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n    const isSun = date.getDay() === 0;\n    const isSat = date.getDay() === 6;\n    const isFirstOfMonth = date.getDate() === 1;\n\n    let className = 'date-header';\n    if (isSun) className += ' is-sunday';\n    if (isSat) className += ' is-saturday';\n    if (holiday) className += ' is-holiday';\n    if (isFirstOfMonth) className += ' month-start';\n\n    return (\n      <div key={`date-${date.toISOString()}`} \n           className={className} \n           style={{ gridColumn: `${dIdx * periods.length + 2} / span ${periods.length}`, gridRow: 1 }}\n           title={holiday?.name}\n      >\n        {dateFormatter.format(date)}\n      </div>\n    );\n  });\n\n  const periodHeaders = displayDates.flatMap((date, dIdx) => \n    periods.map((p, pIdx) => {\n      const isSun = date.getDay() === 0;\n      const isSat = date.getDay() === 6;\n      const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n      let className = 'period-header';\n      if (isSun) className += ' is-sunday';\n      if (isSat) className += ' is-saturday';\n      if (holiday) className += ' is-holiday';\n\n      return (\n        <div key={`period-${date.toISOString()}-${p.id}`} \n             className={className} \n             style={{ gridColumn: dIdx * periods.length + pIdx + 2, gridRow: 2 }}>\n          {p.name}\n        </div>\n      );\n    })\n  );\n\n  const eventLabel = (\n    <div key=\"label-event\" className=\"event-label\" style={{ ...stickyLeft, gridColumn: 1, gridRow: 3 }}>\n      {labels.event}\n    </div>\n  );\n\n  const eventCells = displayDates.flatMap((date, dIdx) => {\n    const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n    const isSun = date.getDay() === 0;\n    const isSat = date.getDay() === 6;\n    let className = 'grid-cell event-cell';\n    if (isSun) className += ' is-sunday';\n    if (isSat) className += ' is-saturday';\n    if (holiday) className += ' is-holiday';\n\n    return periods.map((_, pIdx) => (\n      <div key={`event-cell-${dIdx}-${pIdx}`} \n           className={className} \n           style={{ gridColumn: dIdx * periods.length + pIdx + 2, gridRow: 3 }} />\n    ));\n  });\n\n  // イベント行（row 3）に表示する全アイテムの競合チェック\n  type Placement = { id: string; start: number; end: number; level: number; element: JSX.Element };\n  const row3Placements: Placement[] = [];\n\n  const getPlacementLevel = (start: number, end: number) => {\n    let level = 0;\n    while (true) {\n      const conflict = row3Placements.some(p => p.level === level && !(end < p.start || start > p.end));\n      if (!conflict) return level;\n      level++;\n    }\n  };\n\n  const holidayItems = displayDates.flatMap((date, dIdx) => {\n    const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n    if (!holiday) return [];\n\n    if (holiday.date && isSameDay(date, startOfDay(parseISO(holiday.date)))) {\n      const startCol = dIdx * periods.length + 2;\n      const endCol = dIdx * periods.length + periods.length + 1;\n      const level = getPlacementLevel(startCol, endCol - 1);\n      const el = (\n        <div key={`holiday-${date.toISOString()}`}\n             className=\"event-card holiday-card\"\n             style={{ \n               gridColumn: `${startCol} / ${endCol}`, \n               gridRow: 3,\n               top: `${72 + level * 22}px`\n             }}>\n          {holiday.name}\n        </div>\n      );\n      row3Placements.push({ id: `holiday-${date.toISOString()}`, start: startCol, end: endCol - 1, level, element: el });\n      return [el];\n    }\n    \n    const hStart = holiday.start ? startOfDay(parseISO(holiday.start)) : null;\n    const hEnd = holiday.end ? startOfDay(parseISO(holiday.end)) : null;\n    \n    if (hStart && hEnd) {\n      if (isSameDay(date, hStart) || (isSameDay(date, displayDates[0]) && isAfter(date, hStart) && isBefore(date, hEnd))) {\n        const actualStart = isAfter(hStart, displayDates[0]) ? hStart : displayDates[0];\n        const actualEnd = isBefore(hEnd, displayDates[displayDates.length - 1]) ? hEnd : displayDates[displayDates.length - 1];\n        \n        const sIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, actualStart));\n        const eIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, actualEnd));\n        \n        if (sIdx !== -1 && eIdx !== -1 && isSameDay(date, actualStart)) {\n          const startCol = sIdx * periods.length + 2;\n          const endCol = eIdx * periods.length + periods.length + 1;\n          const level = getPlacementLevel(startCol, endCol - 1);\n          const el = (\n            <div key={`holiday-range-${holiday.name}-${date.toISOString()}`}\n                 className=\"event-card holiday-card\"\n                 style={{ \n                   gridColumn: `${startCol} / ${endCol}`, \n                   gridRow: 3,\n                   top: `${72 + level * 22}px`\n                 }}>\n              {holiday.name}\n            </div>\n          );\n          row3Placements.push({ id: `holiday-range-${holiday.name}`, start: startCol, end: endCol - 1, level, element: el });\n          return [el];\n        }\n      }\n    }\n    \n    return [];\n  });\n\n  const scheduleEventItems = events.flatMap(e => {\n    const eStart = startOfDay(parseISO(e.startDate));\n    const eEnd = startOfDay(parseISO(e.endDate));\n    \n    if (isAfter(eStart, currentViewEnd) || isBefore(eEnd, currentViewStart)) return [];\n\n    const startDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, eStart));\n    const endDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, eEnd));\n    const startPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === e.startPeriodId);\n    const endPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === e.endPeriodId);\n\n    // ビュー外でも一部が掛かっている場合の調整\n    const sCol = (startDayIdx === -1) ? 2 : startDayIdx * periods.length + startPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const eCol = (endDayIdx === -1) ? (displayDates.length * periods.length + 1) : endDayIdx * periods.length + endPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const span = eCol - sCol + 1;\n\n    const result = [];\n    \n    // リソースIDのリストを統合\n    const resourceIdList = [\n      ...(e.resourceIds || []),\n      ...(e.resources || []).map(r => r.id)\n    ];\n\n    // リソース固有の予定\n    if (resourceIdList.length > 0) {\n      resourceIdList.forEach(resId => {\n        const resourceIdx = filteredResources.findIndex(r => r.id === resId);\n        if (resourceIdx !== -1) {\n          result.push(\n            <div key={`event-${e.id}-${resId}`} \n                 className=\"event-card schedule-event-card\"\n                 style={{ \n                   gridColumn: `${sCol} / span ${span}`, \n                   gridRow: resourceIdx + 4,\n                   backgroundColor: e.color\n                 }}>\n              {e.name}\n            </div>\n          );\n        }\n      });\n    }\n\n    // イベント行（row 3）に表示する場合\n    if (e.showInEventRow !== false || resourceIdList.length === 0) {\n      const level = getPlacementLevel(sCol, sCol + span - 1);\n      const el = (\n        <div key={`event-${e.id}-global`} \n             className=\"event-card schedule-event-card\"\n             style={{ \n               gridColumn: `${sCol} / span ${span}`, \n               gridRow: 3,\n               backgroundColor: e.color,\n               top: `${72 + level * 22}px`\n             }}>\n          {e.name}\n        </div>\n      );\n      row3Placements.push({ id: `event-${e.id}`, start: sCol, end: sCol + span - 1, level, element: el });\n      result.push(el);\n    }\n\n    return result;\n  });\n\n  const resourceLabels = filteredResources.map((r, idx) => (\n    <div key={`label-${r.id}`} className=\"grid-label\" style={{ ...stickyLeft, gridColumn: 1, gridRow: idx + 4 }}>\n      {r.name}\n    </div>\n  ));\n\n  const lessonItems = lessons.flatMap(l => {\n    const lStart = startOfDay(parseISO(l.startDate));\n    const lEnd = startOfDay(parseISO(l.endDate));\n\n    if (isAfter(lStart, currentViewEnd) || isBefore(lEnd, currentViewStart)) return [];\n    \n    const startDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, lStart));\n    const endDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, lEnd));\n    const startPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.startPeriodId);\n    const endPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.endPeriodId);\n\n    const sCol = (startDayIdx === -1) ? 2 : startDayIdx * periods.length + startPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const eCol = (endDayIdx === -1) ? (displayDates.length * periods.length + 1) : endDayIdx * periods.length + endPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const span = eCol - sCol + 1;\n\n    const subIds = [\n      ...(l.subTeacherIds || []),\n      ...(l.subTeachers || []).map(t => t.id)\n    ];\n\n    // 関連するリソースIDを特定\n    let targetResIds: string[] = [];\n    if (viewMode === 'room') targetResIds = [l.roomId];\n    else if (viewMode === 'teacher') targetResIds = [l.teacherId, ...subIds];\n    else if (viewMode === 'course') targetResIds = [l.courseId];\n\n    return targetResIds.map(resId => {\n      const resourceIdx = filteredResources.findIndex(r => r.id === resId);\n      if (resourceIdx === -1) return null;\n\n      const infoItems = [];\n      if (viewMode !== 'room') infoItems.push({ label: labels.room, value: getResourceName(l.roomId) });\n      \n      const mainTeacherName = getResourceName(l.teacherId);\n      const subTeacherNames = subIds.map(id => getResourceName(id));\n      \n      if (viewMode !== 'teacher') {\n        const allTeachers = [mainTeacherName, ...subTeacherNames].join(', ');\n        infoItems.push({ label: labels.teacher, value: allTeachers });\n      } else {\n        if (subTeacherNames.length > 0) {\n          // メイン・サブ講師を分けずに表示（同等に扱う）\n          const allTeachers = [mainTeacherName, ...subTeacherNames].join(', ');\n          infoItems.push({ label: labels.teacher, value: allTeachers });\n        }\n      }\n\n      if (viewMode !== 'course') infoItems.push({ label: labels.course, value: getResourceName(l.courseId) });\n      const tooltipText = `${l.subject}\\n` + infoItems.map(item => `${item.label}: ${item.value}`).join('\\n');\n\n      return (\n        <div \n          key={`lesson-${l.id}-${resId}`} \n          className=\"lesson-card\"\n          style={{\n            gridColumn: `${sCol} / span ${span}`,\n            gridRow: resourceIdx + 4\n          }}\n          title={tooltipText}\n        >\n          <div className=\"lesson-subject\">{l.subject}</div>\n          <div className=\"lesson-details\">\n            {infoItems.map((item, idx) => (\n              <div key={idx} className=\"lesson-info\">\n                {item.label}: {item.value}\n              </div>\n            ))}\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      );\n    }).filter(Boolean);\n  });\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"timetable-wrapper\">\n      <div \n        key={`grid-${viewType}-${baseDate.getTime()}-${viewMode}-${filteredResources.length}-${totalCols}`}\n        className=\"timetable-container\" \n        style={gridStyle}\n      >\n        <div className=\"grid-corner\" style={{ ...stickyLeft, gridColumn: 1, gridRow: \"1 / span 2\", zIndex: 30 }} />\n        {filteredResources.map((_, rIdx) => \n          displayDates.map((date, dIdx) => {\n            const isSun = date.getDay() === 0;\n            const isSat = date.getDay() === 6;\n            const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n            let cellClass = 'grid-cell';\n            if (isSun) cellClass += ' is-sunday';\n            if (isSat) cellClass += ' is-saturday';\n            if (holiday) cellClass += ' is-holiday';\n            return periods.map((_, pIdx) => (\n              <div key={`cell-${rIdx}-${dIdx}-${pIdx}`} \n                   className={cellClass} \n                   style={{ gridColumn: dIdx * periods.length + pIdx + 2, gridRow: rIdx + 4 }} />\n            ));\n          })\n        )}\n        {dateHeaders}\n        {periodHeaders}\n        {eventLabel}\n        {eventCells}\n        {/* レベル別の配置を確保 */}\n        {holidayItems}\n        {scheduleEventItems}\n        {resourceLabels}\n        {lessonItems}\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n",
    "file_path": "src/components/Timetable.tsx"
  }
}
```
